Chapter_Header: 1
Verse_Ch: 1:1 便雅悯地亚拿突城的祭司中，希勒家的儿子耶利米的话记在下面。 ###EN### The words of Jeremiah the son of Hilkiah, of the priests who were in Anathoth in the land of Benjamin,
Verse_Ch: 1:2 犹大王亚们的儿子约西亚在位第十三年，耶和华的话临到耶利米。 ###EN### To whom the word of Jehovah came in the days of Josiah the son of Amon the king of Judah, in the thirteenth year of his reign.
Verse_Ch: 1:3 从犹大王约西亚的儿子约雅敬在位的日子，直到犹大王约西亚的儿子西底家在位的末年，就是第十一年五月间，耶路撒冷人被掳的时候，耶和华的话 也常临到耶利米。 ###EN### It came also in the days of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah the king of Judah until the end of the eleventh year of Zedekiah the son of Josiah the king of Judah, until the captivity of Jerusalem in the fifth month.
Verse_Ch: 1:4 耶和华的话临到我，说： ###EN### Now the word of Jehovah came to me, saying:
Verse_Ch: 1:5 我未将你造在母腹中，我已晓得你；你未出母胎，我已将你分别为圣；我已派你作列国的申言者。 ###EN### Before I formed you in the womb, I knew you; And before you came forth from the womb, I sanctified you. I have appointed you as a prophet to the nations.
Verse_Ch: 1:6 我就说，主耶和华阿！哎，我不知怎样说，因为我是年幼的。 ###EN### Then I said, Alas, Lord Jehovah! Indeed, I do not know how to speak, For I am a youth.
Verse_Ch: 1:7 耶和华对我说，你不要说我是年幼的；因为我差遣你到谁那里去，你都要去；我吩咐你说什么话，你都要说。 ###EN### But Jehovah said to me, Do not say, I am a youth; For everywhere I send you, you shall go; And everything I command you, you shall speak.
Verse_Ch: 1:8 你不要惧怕他们的面，因为我与你同在，要拯救你；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### Do not be afraid of their faces, For I am with you to deliver you, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 1:9 于是耶和华伸手触我的口；耶和华对我说，我已将我的话放在你口中。 ###EN### Then Jehovah stretched out His hand and touched my mouth; and Jehovah said to me, Now I have put My words in your mouth.
Verse_Ch: 1:10 看哪，我今日派你在列邦列国之上，为要拔出并拆毁，毁坏并倾覆，建造并栽植。 ###EN### See, I have appointed you this day Over the nations and over the kingdoms To pluck up and to break down, To destroy and to tear down, To build up and to plant.
Verse_Ch: 1:11 耶和华的话又临到我，说，耶利米，你看见什么？我说，我看见一根杏树枝。 ###EN### Then the word of Jehovah came to me, saying, What do you see, Jeremiah? And I said, I see a branch of an almond tree.
Verse_Ch: 1:12 耶和华对我说，你看得不错；因为我留意我的话，使其成就。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to me, You have seen well, for I am watching over My word to perform it.
Verse_Ch: 1:13 耶和华的话第二次临到我，说，你看见什么？我说，我看见一个烧开的锅，从北而倾。 ###EN### Then the word of Jehovah came to me a second time, saying, What do you see? And I said, I see a boiling pot, and it is facing away from the north.
Verse_Ch: 1:14 耶和华对我说，必有灾祸从北方发出，临到这地的一切居民。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to me, Out of the north evil will be let loose upon all the inhabitants of the land.
Verse_Ch: 1:15 耶和华说，我要召北方列国的众族；他们要来，各安座位在耶路撒冷的城门口，周围攻击城墙，又要攻击犹大的一切城邑。 ###EN### For I am now calling all the families from the kingdoms of the north, declares Jehovah, and they will come and set each one his throne at the entrance of the gates of Jerusalem and against all its walls all around and against all the cities of Judah.
Verse_Ch: 1:16 至于这民的一切恶，就是离弃我，向别神献祭，跪拜自己手所造的，我要向他们发出我的判语。 ###EN### And I will utter My judgment on them concerning all their wickedness by which they have forsaken Me and have offered sacrifices to other gods and have worshipped the works of their own hands.
Verse_Ch: 1:17 所以你当束腰，起来将我所吩咐你的一切话告诉他们；不要因他们惊惶，免得我使你在他们面前惊惶。 ###EN### You therefore gird up your loins, and rise up and speak to them everything that I command you. Do not be dismayed before them, lest I dismay you in their presence.
Verse_Ch: 1:18 我今日使你成为坚城、铁柱、铜墙，抵挡全地，就是抵挡犹大的君王、首领、祭司、并这地的众民。 ###EN### And I am now making you today into a fortified city and into an iron pillar and into bronze walls against the whole land, against the kings of Judah, against its princes, against its priests, and against the people of the land.
Verse_Ch: 1:19 他们要攻击你，却不能胜过你；因为我与你同在，要拯救你；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### And they will fight against you, but they will not prevail against you; for I am with you, declares Jehovah, to deliver you.
Chapter_Header: 2
Verse_Ch: 2:1 耶和华的话临到我，说， ###EN### And the word of Jehovah came to me, saying,
Verse_Ch: 2:2 你去向耶路撒冷人的耳中喊叫，说，耶和华如此说，你幼年的恩爱，新婚的爱情，你怎样在旷野，在未曾耕种之地跟随我，我都记得。 ###EN### Go and cry in the ears of Jerusalem, saying, Thus says Jehovah: I remember concerning you the kindness of your youth, The love of your bridal days, When you followed after Me in the wilderness, In a land that was not sown.
Verse_Ch: 2:3 那时以色列归耶和华为圣，作为祂所出产的初熟果子；凡吞吃他的，便算为有罪，灾祸就临到他们；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### Israel was holiness to Jehovah, The firstfruits of His increase; All who ate of it were guilty; Evil came upon them, Declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 2:4 雅各家，以色列家的各族阿，你们当听耶和华的话。 ###EN### Hear the word of Jehovah, O house of Jacob and all the families of the house of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 2:5 耶和华如此说，你们的列祖见我有什么不义，竟远离我，随从虚无的神，自己成为虚妄呢？ ###EN### Thus says Jehovah: What iniquity did your fathers find in Me That they went far away from Me And walked after vanity And became vain?
Verse_Ch: 2:6 他们也不说，那领我们从埃及地上来，引导我们经过旷野，经过沙漠有深坑之地，经过干旱死荫之地，经过无人通行、无人居住之地的耶和华在那里 呢？ ###EN### And they did not say, Where is Jehovah, Who brought us up from the land of Egypt, Who brought us through the wilderness, Through a land of deserts and pits, Through a land of drought and the shadow of death, Through a land that no one passes through And where no man dwells?
Verse_Ch: 2:7 我领你们进入肥美之地，使你们得吃其中的果子和美物；但你们进入的时候，就玷污我的地，使我的产业成为可憎之物。 ###EN### And I brought you into the land of the fruited field, To eat its fruit and its goodness. But you came and defiled My land And made My inheritance an abomination.
Verse_Ch: 2:8 祭司都不说，耶和华在那里呢？执掌律法的，都不认识我，牧者违背我，申言者藉巴力说预言，随从无益之物。 ###EN### The priests did not say, Where is Jehovah? And those who handle the law did not know Me, And the shepherds transgressed against Me, And the prophets prophesied by Baal And followed after things that did not benefit them.
Verse_Ch: 2:9 耶和华说，因此我必与你们争辩，也必与你们的子孙争辩。 ###EN### Therefore I will yet contend with you, declares Jehovah; And with your children's children I will contend.
Verse_Ch: 2:10 你们且过到基提众海岛去察看，打发人往基达去留心查考，看曾有这样的事没有。 ###EN### For pass over to the coastlands of Kittim and see, And send someone to Kedar and consider carefully, And see if there has ever been anything like this.
Verse_Ch: 2:11 岂有一国换了自己的神么？其实那些并不是神；但我的百姓，将他们的荣耀换了那无益的神。 ###EN### Has a nation ever exchanged its gods, Even though they are no gods? But My people have exchanged their glory For that which does not benefit them.
Verse_Ch: 2:12 诸天哪，要因此惊骇、恐慌，极其凄凉；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### Be appalled at this, O heavens, And be horrified; be very desolate, Declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 2:13 因为我的百姓，作了两件恶事，就是离弃我这活水的泉源，为自己凿出池子，是破裂不能存水的池子。 ###EN### For My people have committed two evils: They have forsaken Me, The fountain of living waters, To hew out for themselves cisterns, Broken cisterns, Which hold no water.
Verse_Ch: 2:14 以色列是奴仆么？是家中生的奴仆么？为何竟成为掠物呢？ ###EN### Is Israel a slave? Is he a homeborn slave? Why has he become a prey?
Verse_Ch: 2:15 少壮狮子向他咆哮，大发吼声，使他的地荒凉，城邑也都焚烧，无人居住。 ###EN### The young lions roared over him; They sounded their voices. And they have made his land a waste; His cities are burned, without inhabitant.
Verse_Ch: 2:16 挪弗人和答比匿人，也剃光你的头顶。 ###EN### Also the children of Memphis and Tahpanhes Have shaved the crown of your head.
Verse_Ch: 2:17 这事临到你身上，不是你自招的么？不是因耶和华你神引你行路的时候，你离弃了祂么？ ###EN### Have you not done this to yourself By your forsaking Jehovah your God When He was leading you in the way?
Verse_Ch: 2:18 现今你为何在往埃及的路上，要喝西曷的水呢？你为何在往亚述的路上，要喝大河的水呢？ ###EN### And now what do you have on the road to Egypt, To drink the waters of the Shihor? And what do you have on the road to Assyria, To drink the waters of the River?
Verse_Ch: 2:19 你自己的恶必惩治你，你背道的事必责备你。因此要知道并看见，你离弃耶和华你的神，对我毫无畏惧，乃为恶事，为苦事；这是主万军之耶和华说 的。 ###EN### Your own wickedness will correct you, And your apostasies will reprove you. Know therefore and see that it is an evil and bitter thing, That you have forsaken Jehovah your God And that My fear is not in you, Declares the Lord Jehovah of hosts.
Verse_Ch: 2:20 你在古时折断你的轭，挣开你的绳索；你说，我必不事奉耶和华！你在各高冈上，各青翠树下，躺卧行淫。 ###EN### For long ago you broke your yoke; You tore off your bonds; And you said, I will not serve! Indeed upon every high hill And under every flourishing tree You have lain down, you have committed fornication.
Verse_Ch: 2:21 然而我栽种你是上好的葡萄树，全然是真种子。你怎么向我变为外邦葡萄树的坏枝条呢？ ###EN### Yet I, I had planted you as a choice vine, Wholly a faithful seed. How then have you turned yourself before Me Into the degenerate shoots of a foreign vine?
Verse_Ch: 2:22 你虽用碱，多用肥皂洗濯，你罪孽的污渍仍然留在我面前；这是主耶和华说的。 ###EN### For though you wash yourself with lye And make use of much soap, Your iniquity remains as a stain before Me, Declares the Lord Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 2:23 你怎能说，我没有被玷污，没有随从众巴力？看你谷中的路，就知道你所作的如何。你像快行的小骆驼，狂奔乱走； ###EN### How can you say, I am not defiled; I have not gone after the Baals? Look at your way in the valley; Know what you have done. You are like a swift young camel entangling her ways,
Verse_Ch: 2:24 你像野母驴惯在旷野，欲心发动就吸风喘气。她起性的时候，谁能使她转回呢？凡寻找她的，必不至疲乏：在她的月分，必能寻见。 ###EN### Like a wild donkey accustomed to the wilderness, Panting after the wind in her desire. In her passion who can turn her away? None that seek her will weary themselves: They will find her in her month.
Verse_Ch: 2:25 我说，你不要使脚上无鞋，喉咙干渴；你倒说，这是枉然。我喜爱外邦神，我必随从他们。 ###EN### Keep your foot from being unshod And your throat from thirst; But you said, It is hopeless. No! For I have loved strangers, And I will go after them.
Verse_Ch: 2:26 贼被捉拿，怎样羞愧，以色列家和他们的君王、首领、祭司、申言者，也照样羞愧。 ###EN### As the thief is ashamed when he is found, So the house of Israel is ashamed-They, their kings, their princes, And their priests and their prophets,
Verse_Ch: 2:27 他们向树木说，你是我的父；向石头说，你生了我。他们以背向着我，不以面向着我；及至遭遇患难的时候却说，起来拯救我们。 ###EN### Who say to a tree, You are my father; And to a stone, You have brought me forth-For they have turned their back to Me, And not their faces. Yet in a time of their trouble they will say, Arise and save us.
Verse_Ch: 2:28 你为自己作的神在那里？你遭遇患难的时候，他们若能拯救你，就叫他们起来罢。犹大阿，你神的数目，与你城的数目相等。 ###EN### But where are your gods, whom you made for yourselves? Let them arise, if they can save you in the time of your trouble; For according to the number of your cities Are your gods, O Judah.
Verse_Ch: 2:29 耶和华说，你们为何与我争辩？你们都违背了我。 ###EN### Why do you contend with Me? You have all transgressed against Me, Declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 2:30 我责打你们的儿女，是徒然的：他们不受管教；你们自己的刀，吞灭你们的申言者，好像残害的狮子。 ###EN### In vain I have stricken your children: They have taken no correction. Your own sword has devoured your prophets Like a destroying lion.
Verse_Ch: 2:31 这世代的人哪，你们要注意耶和华的话：我岂向以色列成了旷野么？或成了幽暗之地么？我的百姓为何说，我们自由无拘，再不来你这里了？ ###EN### O generation, attend to the word of Jehovah: Have I been a wilderness to Israel, Or a land of deep darkness? Why do My people say, We roam about; We will no longer come to You?
Verse_Ch: 2:32 处女岂能忘记她的妆饰呢？新妇岂能忘记她的美衣呢？我的百姓，却忘记了我无数的日子。 ###EN### Can the virgin forget her ornaments, Or the bride her attire? But My people have forgotten Me For days without number.
Verse_Ch: 2:33 你多么会修饰自己的道路，去寻求爱情！所以连恶劣的妇人，你也教导她们行你的路。 ###EN### How you prepare your ways To seek love! Therefore ou have even taught Wicked women your ways.
Verse_Ch: 2:34 并且你的衣襟上有无辜穷人的血；你杀他们，并不是遇见他们挖洞入屋，乃是因这一切的事。 ###EN### Also on your skirts is found The lifeblood of the innocent poor. You did not find them breaking in, But killed them because of all these things.
Verse_Ch: 2:35 你还说，我是无辜的；耶和华的怒气，必定从我转消了。我必审问你，因你说，我没有犯罪。 ###EN### But you said, I am innocent; Surely His anger will turn from me. I am about to enter into judgment with you, Because you say, I have not sinned.
Verse_Ch: 2:36 你为何东奔西跑，更换你的道路呢？你也必因埃及蒙羞，像从前因亚述蒙羞一样。 ###EN### Why do you go about so much To change your way? You will be put to shame by Egypt also, Even as you were put to shame by Assyria.
Verse_Ch: 2:37 你必两手抱头，从埃及出来；因为耶和华已经弃绝你所倚靠的，你必不因他们得亨通。 ###EN### Indeed, from it you will go forth With your hands upon your head; For Jehovah has rejected those in whom you trust, And you will not prosper by them.
Chapter_Header: 3
Verse_Ch: 3:1 有话说，人若休妻，妻子离他而去，作了别人的妻子，前夫岂能再回到她那里么？若回到她那里，那地岂不是大大污秽了么？但你和许多所爱的人行 邪淫，还可以归向我；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### It is said, If a man divorces his wife And she goes from him And becomes another man's wife, Will he return to her again? Will not that land be Utterly polluted? But you have committed fornication with many lovers. et return to Me, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 3:2 你向光秃的高处举目观看：你在何处没有被玷污？你坐在道旁等候他们，好像亚拉伯人在荒野埋伏一样；你以你的淫行邪恶污秽了这地。 ###EN### Lift up your eyes to the bare heights and see: Where have you not been ravished? By the roads you sat for them, Like an Arab in the desert; And you have polluted the land With your fornication and your wickedness.
Verse_Ch: 3:3 因此甘霖停止，春雨不降。但你还是有娼妓之脸，不顾羞耻。 ###EN### Therefore the showers have been withheld, And there has been no spring rain. But you have had a harlot's forehead; You refused to be ashamed.
Verse_Ch: 3:4 你岂不是刚刚向我呼叫说，我父阿，你是我幼年时的引导么？ ###EN### Have you not just now called out to Me, My Father, You are the guide of my youth?
Verse_Ch: 3:5 耶和华岂永远怀怒，存留到底么？你虽这样说，还是尽所能的作恶事。 ###EN### Will He preserve His anger forever? Will He keep it perpetually? This you have spoken; yet you have done what evil things That you could.
Verse_Ch: 3:6 约西亚王在位的日子，耶和华又对我说，背道的以色列所行的，你看见没有？她上各高山，在各青翠树下行淫。 ###EN### Then Jehovah said to me in the days of Josiah the king, Have you seen what Israel the apostate has done? She went up on every high mountain and under every flourishing tree and committed fornication there.
Verse_Ch: 3:7 我说，她行这一切事以后，必归向我；她却不归向我；她奸诈的妹妹犹大也看见了。 ###EN### And I said, After she has done all these things, she will return to Me; but she did not return, and her treacherous sister Judah saw it.
Verse_Ch: 3:8 因背道的以色列所犯的一切奸淫，我给她休书休了她；但她奸诈的妹妹犹大还不惧怕，也去行淫。 ###EN### And I saw that because of all the adultery that Israel the apostate committed I divorced her and gave her a certificate of divorce, yet her sister Judah the treacherous did not fear but went and committed fornication also.
Verse_Ch: 3:9 因以色列轻忽她的淫乱，和石头木头行淫，就污秽了这地。 ###EN### And because she treated her fornication lightly, she polluted the land and committed adultery with stones and trees.
Verse_Ch: 3:10 虽有这一切的事，她奸诈的妹妹犹大，还不全心归向我，不过是假意归向我；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### And yet in spite of all this her treacherous sister Judah did not return to Me with all her heart, but instead falsely, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 3:11 耶和华对我说，背道的以色列，比奸诈的犹大还显为义。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to me, Israel the apostate has shown herself to be more righteous than Judah the treacherous.
Verse_Ch: 3:12 你去向北方宣告这些话，说，耶和华说，背道的以色列阿，回来罢；我必不向你们变脸；因为我是有怜悯的，我必不永远存怒；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### Go and proclaim these words to the north, and say, Return, O Israel the apostate, declares Jehovah; And I will not let My countenance fall toward you; For I am merciful, declares Jehovah; I will not keep My anger forever.
Verse_Ch: 3:13 只要承认你的罪孽，就是你违背了耶和华你的神，在各青翠树下，向外邦神东奔西跑，没有听从我的话；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### Only acknowledge your iniquity, That you have transgressed against Jehovah your God And have turned your ways here and there to strangers under every flourishing tree, And have not listened to My voice, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 3:14 耶和华说，背道的儿女阿，回来罢，因为我是你们的丈夫；并且我必将你们从一城取一人，从一族取两人，将你们带到锡安。 ###EN### Return, O apostate children, declares Jehovah, for I am a Husband to you; and I will take you, one from a city and two from a family, and will bring you to Zion.
Verse_Ch: 3:15 我也必将合乎我心的牧者赐给你们；他们必以知识和明智，牧养你们。 ###EN### And I will give you shepherds according to My own heart, who will feed you knowledge and understanding.
Verse_Ch: 3:16 耶和华说，你们在这地繁衍增多，当那些日子，人必不再题说，耶和华的约柜！他们不追想，不记念，不觉缺少，也不再制造。 ###EN### And when you are multiplied and increased in the land, in those days, declares Jehovah, they will no longer say, The Ark of the Covenant of Jehovah! And it will not come to mind, nor will they remember it or visit it; and it will not be made again.
Verse_Ch: 3:17 那时，人必称耶路撒冷为耶和华的宝座；万国必聚集到那里，因为耶和华的名在耶路撒冷；他们必不再随从自己顽梗的恶心行事。 ###EN### At that time they will call Jerusalem the throne of Jehovah, and all the nations will be gathered to it because the name of Jehovah is at Jerusalem; and they will no longer walk after the stubbornness of their evil heart.
Verse_Ch: 3:18 当那些日子，犹大家要和以色列家同行，从北方之地，一同来到我赐给他们列祖为业之地。 ###EN### In those days the house of Judah will walk with the house of Israel, and they will come together from the land of the north to the land which I have given to their fathers as an inheritance.
Verse_Ch: 3:19 我说，我多么愿意将你安置在众子之中，赐给你可悦之地，就是万国中极佳美的产业！我又说，你们必称我为父，也不再转去不跟从我。 ###EN### But I said, How I will put you among the sons, And give you a pleasant land, An inheritance of the most ornate of the nations! And I said, You will call Me, My Father, And will not turn away from Me.
Verse_Ch: 3:20 以色列家阿，你们向我行诡诈，真像妇人行诡诈，离开她丈夫一样；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### Surely as a woman acts treacherously by departing from her husband, So you have dealt treacherously with Me, O house of Israel, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 3:21 在光秃的高处听见声音，就是以色列人哭泣恳求之声；因为他们走了弯曲的道路，忘记了耶和华他们的神。 ###EN### A voice is heard on the bare heights, The weeping, the supplications, of the children of Israel; For they have perverted their way; They have forgotten Jehovah their God.
Verse_Ch: 3:22 背道的儿女阿，回来罢；我要医治你们背道的病。我们来到你这里，因你是耶和华我们的神。 ###EN### Return, O apostate children; I will heal you of your apostasies. Now we come to You, For You are Jehovah our God.
Verse_Ch: 3:23 仰望从小山，或从大山的喧嚷中得帮助，真是枉然。以色列得拯救，诚然在于耶和华我们的神。 ###EN### Surely in vain have we hoped for anything from the hills; The mountains are a tumult; Surely in Jehovah our God Is the salvation of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 3:24 从我们幼年以来，那可耻的偶像，已将我们列祖所劳碌得来的羊群、牛群、和他们的儿女，都吞吃了。 ###EN### But shame has devoured the labor of our fathers since our youth, their flocks and their herds, their sons and their daughters.
Verse_Ch: 3:25 我们在自己的羞耻中躺卧罢；愿惭愧将我们遮盖；因为我们和我们的列祖，从幼年直到今日，常常得罪耶和华我们的神，没有听从耶和华我们神的话。 ###EN### Let us lie down in our shame, and let our humiliation cover us; for we have sinned against Jehovah our God, we and our fathers, since our youth even unto this day; and we have not listened to the voice of Jehovah our God.
Chapter_Header: 4
Verse_Ch: 4:1 耶和华说，以色列阿，你若回来，就当回到我这里；你若从我面前除掉你可憎之物，不四处游荡， ###EN### If you will return, O Israel, declares Jehovah, Return to Me; And if you put away your detestable things from My presence And do not wander,
Verse_Ch: 4:2 并且凭真实、公平、公义，指着永活的耶和华起誓，列国就必凭耶和华称自己为有福，也必凭祂夸耀。 ###EN### And swear, As Jehovah lives, In truth and in justice and in righteousness, Then the nations will bless themselves in Him, And in Him they will glory.
Verse_Ch: 4:3 耶和华对犹大和耶路撒冷人如此说，要开垦你们未耕之地，不要撒种在荆棘中。 ###EN### For thus says Jehovah to the men of Judah and to Jerusalem, Break up your fallow ground, And do not sow among thorns.
Verse_Ch: 4:4 犹大人和耶路撒冷的居民哪，你们当自行割礼，归耶和华，将心里的污秽除掉；恐怕我的忿怒，因你们的恶行发作，如火焚烧，无人能以熄灭。 ###EN### Circumcise yourselves to Jehovah, And remove the foreskins of your heart, Men of Judah and inhabitants of Jerusalem, Lest My wrath go forth like fire And burn, and there be no one to quench it Because of the evil of your deeds.
Verse_Ch: 4:5 你们当传扬在犹大，宣告在耶路撒冷，说，你们当在这地吹角，高声呼叫说，你们当聚集，我们好进入坚固城。 ###EN### Declare in Judah And proclaim in Jerusalem, and say: Blow the trumpet in the land; Cry aloud and say, Gather yourselves and let us go Into the fortified cities.
Verse_Ch: 4:6 应当向锡安竖立旌旗；要逃避，不要停留；因我必使灾祸，与大毁灭，从北方来到。 ###EN### Raise up a standard toward Zion. Seek refuge; do not stay; For I am bringing evil from the north, And great destruction.
Verse_Ch: 4:7 有狮子已经从树丛中上来，毁坏列国的已经动身。他已经出离本处，要使你的地荒凉；你的城邑必变为荒场，无人居住。 ###EN### A lion has come up from his thicket, And a destroyer of nations has set out. He has gone forth from his place To make your land a waste; Your cities will be ruins, Without an inhabitant.
Verse_Ch: 4:8 因此，你们当腰束麻布，恸哭哀号；因为耶和华的烈怒，没有转离我们。 ###EN### For this, gird yourselves with sackcloth, Wail and howl; For the burning anger of Jehovah Has not turned away from us.
Verse_Ch: 4:9 耶和华说，到那日君王和首领的心，都要沮丧；祭司都要惊奇，申言者都要诧异。 ###EN### And in that day, declares Jehovah, the heart of the king and the heart of the princes will fail; and the priests will be appalled, and the prophets will be astounded.
Verse_Ch: 4:10 我说，哀哉，主耶和华阿，你真是大大的欺哄了这百姓和耶路撒冷，说，你们必得平安；其实刀剑害及性命了。 ###EN### And I said, Alas, Lord Jehovah, surely You have utterly deceived this people and Jerusalem, saying, You will have peace; whereas the sword reaches to the soul.
Verse_Ch: 4:11 那时，必有话对这百姓和耶路撒冷说，有一阵热风，从旷野光秃的高处，向我的百姓刮来，不是为簸扬，也不是为扬净； ###EN### At that time it will be said to this people and to Jerusalem, A hot wind from the bare heights in the wilderness toward the daughter of My people, not for winnowing nor for purging
Verse_Ch: 4:12 这一阵风强烈难当，从我刮到；现在我又必发出判语，攻击他们。 ( ###EN### A wind too strong for these), will come from Me; now I will also utter judgments against them.
Verse_Ch: 4:13 他必如云上来，他的战车如旋风，他的马比鹰更快。我们有祸了，我们遭殃了！ ###EN### Here he is coming up like clouds, And his chariots like the whirlwind; His horses are swifter than eagles. Woe to us for we are devastated!
Verse_Ch: 4:14 耶路撒冷阿，你当洗去心中的恶，使你可以得救；恶念存留在你心里，要到几时呢？ ###EN### Wash your heart from wickedness, O Jerusalem, That you may be saved. How long will your evil thoughts Lodge within you?
Verse_Ch: 4:15 有声音从但宣扬，从以法莲山地报患难。 ###EN### For a voice declares from Dan And announces affliction from the hill country of Ephraim.
Verse_Ch: 4:16 你们当向列国题说，向耶路撒冷报告，说，有围困的人从远方来到，向犹大的城邑发声呐喊。 ###EN### Make mention to the nations; yes, Announce against Jerusalem. Besiegers are coming from a distant land And utter their voice against the cities of Judah.
Verse_Ch: 4:17 他们四面围住耶路撒冷，好像看守田地的人，因为她背叛了我；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### Like those who watch over a field, they are against her all around Because she has rebelled against Me, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 4:18 你的行径，你的作为，给你招惹这些事；这是你的恶果；实在是苦，是害及你心了！ ###EN### Your way and your deeds Have caused these things to happen to you. This is your wickedness. Indeed it is bitter! Indeed it reaches to your heart!
Verse_Ch: 4:19 我的心肠阿，我的心肠阿，我翻腾绞痛。我的心哪！我的心在我里面呻吟；我不能静默不言；因为我的魂哪，你已经听见角声，听见打仗的呐喊。 ###EN### My bowels, my bowels; I am writhing. O the walls of my heart! My heart is moaning within me; I cannot be silent; For you hear, O my soul, the sound of the trumpet, The alarm of war.
Verse_Ch: 4:20 毁坏的信息接连不断，因为全地败落；我的帐棚忽然破败，我的幔子顷刻破裂。 ###EN### Destruction upon destruction is proclaimed, For the whole land is devastated. Suddenly my tents are devastated, And my curtains in a moment.
Verse_Ch: 4:21 我看见旌旗，听见角声，要到几时呢？ ###EN### How long will I see the standard, And hear the sound of the trumpet?
Verse_Ch: 4:22 耶和华说，我的百性愚顽，不认识我。他们是愚蠢无知的儿女；他们有智慧行恶，却无知识行善。 ###EN### For My people are foolish; They do not know Me. They are stupid children And have no understanding. They are wise to do evil, But they do not know to do good.
Verse_Ch: 4:23 申言者说，我观看地，见地荒废空虚；我观看天，天也无光。 ###EN### I looked at the earth, and there it was, waste and emptiness; And at the heavens, and they had no light.
Verse_Ch: 4:24 我观看大山，见大山尽都震动，小山也都摇来摇去。 ###EN### I looked at the mountains, and there they were, shaking, And all the hills were swaying.
Verse_Ch: 4:25 我观看，见无一人，空中的飞鸟也都躲避。 ###EN### I looked, and there was no man, And all the birds of the heavens had fled.
Verse_Ch: 4:26 我观看，见肥田变为荒野，一切城邑在耶和华面前，在祂烈怒之前，都被拆毁。 ###EN### I looked, and there was the fruitful land, a wilderness, And all its cities were torn down Before Jehovah, before His burning anger.
Verse_Ch: 4:27 耶和华如此说，全地必然荒凉，我却不毁灭净尽。 ###EN### For thus says Jehovah, The whole land will be a desolation, But I will not make a full end;
Verse_Ch: 4:28 为此，地要悲哀，在上的天也必黑暗；因为我言已出，我意已定；我不后悔，也不转意不作。 ###EN### For this the earth will mourn, And the heavens above will be dark; Because I have spoken, I have purposed; And I have not repented, nor will I turn from it.
Verse_Ch: 4:29 各城的人，因马兵和弓箭手的响声，就都逃跑，进入丛林，爬上磐石。各城被撇下，无一人住在其中。 ###EN### At the sound of horsemen and archers Every city flees; They go into the thickets And climb up on the rocks. Every city is forsaken, And not even one inhabits them.
Verse_Ch: 4:30 你这荒凉的阿，你要怎样行呢？你虽穿上朱红衣服，佩戴黄金妆饰，用颜料修饰眼目，你美化自己是枉然的；你的爱人藐视你，他们寻索你的性命。 ###EN### And you, O desolate one, what will you do? Although you dress in scarlet, Although you are adorned with ornaments of gold, Although you enlarge your eyes with paint, In vain do you beautify yourself; Your lovers despise you; They seek your life.
Verse_Ch: 4:31 我听见有声音，仿佛妇人产难的声音，好像生头胎疼痛的声音，是锡安女子的声音；她喘着气，伸出双手，说，我有祸了，在杀人者跟前，我的魂发 昏了。 ###EN### For I heard a cry like that of a woman in travail, Anguish like that of a woman bringing forth her first child, The sound of the daughter of Zion gasping for breath; She stretches out her hands, saying, Woe is me, For my soul is fainting before murderers.
Chapter_Header: 5
Verse_Ch: 5:1 你们当在耶路撒冷的街上，跑来跑去，观看察知，并在宽阔处寻找，是否有一人施行公理，寻求忠信；若有，我就赦免这城。 ###EN### Go to and fro in the streets of Jerusalem, And look now and know, And seek in her open squares If you can find a man, If there is anyone who executes justice, Who seeks faithfulness; And I will pardon her.
Verse_Ch: 5:2 他们虽然说，我指着永活的耶和华起誓，其实他们所起的誓是假的。 ###EN### And although they say, As Jehovah lives, Nevertheless they swear falsely.
Verse_Ch: 5:3 耶和华阿，你的眼目不是看顾忠信么？你击打他们，他们却不伤恸；你毁灭他们，他们却不受管教。他们使脸刚硬过于磐石，不肯回头。 ###EN### O Jehovah, are not Your eyes upon faithfulness? You have stricken them, But they did not writhe; You have consumed them, But they refused to take correction. They have made their faces harder than rock; They have refused to turn.
Verse_Ch: 5:4 我说，这些人实在是贫穷的，是愚昧的；因为他们不晓得耶和华的法则，和他们神的典章。 ###EN### Then I said, But they are the poor; They are foolish; For they do not know the way of Jehovah, The ordinance of their God.
Verse_Ch: 5:5 我要去见尊大的人，对他们说话；他们必然晓得耶和华的法则，和他们神的典章；但这些人一起将轭折断，挣开绳索。 ###EN### I will go to the great And speak with them; Surely these know the way of Jehovah, The ordinance of their God. But together they both have broken the yoke; They have torn off the bonds.
Verse_Ch: 5:6 因此，林中的狮子必袭击他们，荒地的豺狼必毁灭他们。豹子要窥伺他们的城，凡出城的必被撕碎；因为他们的过犯极多，背道的事也大大加增。 ###EN### Therefore a lion from the forest will strike them; A wolf of the deserts will destroy them. A leopard is watching their cities; Everyone who goes out from them will be torn in pieces; Because they multiplied their transgressions, And their apostasies are great in number.
Verse_Ch: 5:7 我怎能赦免你呢？你的儿女离弃了我，又指着那不是神的起誓。我使他们饱足，他们就行奸淫，成群的到娼妓家里。 ###EN### Why should I pardon you? Your children have forsaken Me And sworn by those who are not gods. When I fed them to the full, they committed adultery And trooped to the house of harlots.
Verse_Ch: 5:8 他们像喂饱的马，到处乱跑，各向邻舍的妻子发嘶声。 ###EN### Like well-fed horses they roam about, Each one neighing after his neighbor's wife.
Verse_Ch: 5:9 耶和华说，我岂不因这些事讨罪呢？我魂岂不报复这样的国呢？ ###EN### Shall I not punish because of these things? Declares Jehovah; And on a nation such as this Shall My soul not avenge itself?
Verse_Ch: 5:10 你们要上去，穿过她葡萄树的行列，施行毁坏；但不可毁坏净尽，只要除掉她的枝子，因为那些不属于耶和华。 ###EN### Go up through her vine rows and destroy, But do not make a full end; Strip away her branches, For they are not Jehovah's.
Verse_Ch: 5:11 原来以色列家和犹大家，对我大行诡诈；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### For the house of Israel and the house of Judah Have dealt very treacherously with Me, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 5:12 他们否认耶和华，说，这并不是祂；灾祸必不临到我们，我们也必不至见到刀剑和饥荒。 ###EN### They have denied Jehovah And have said, He is not; And evil will not come upon us, Nor will we see sword and famine;
Verse_Ch: 5:13 申言者必成为风，话也不在他们里面；因此，这灾必临到他们。 ###EN### And the prophets will become wind, And the word is not in them; Thus it will be done to them.
Verse_Ch: 5:14 所以耶和华万军之神如此说，因为他们说这话，我必使我的话，在你口中为火，使这百姓为柴；这火必将他们吞灭。 ###EN### Therefore thus says Jehovah The God of hosts: Because they have spoken this word, I am now making My words A fire in your mouth, And this people wood; And it will consume them.
Verse_Ch: 5:15 耶和华说，以色列家阿，我必使一国从远方来攻击你，是强盛不衰的国，是从古而有的国；这国的言语你不晓得，他们说的话你不明白。 ###EN### I am now bringing upon you A nation from afar, O house of Israel, declares Jehovah. It is an enduring nation, It is an ancient nation; A nation whose language you do not know, Nor can you understand what they say.
Verse_Ch: 5:16 他们的箭袋，如同敞开的坟墓；他们都是勇士。 ###EN### Their quiver is like an open grave; All of them are mighty men.
Verse_Ch: 5:17 他们必吃尽你的庄稼和你的粮食，吃尽你的儿女；他们必吃尽你的牛群羊群，吃尽你的葡萄树和无花果树；又必用刀毁坏你所倚靠的坚固城。 ###EN### And they will eat up your harvest and your bread; They will eat up your sons and your daughters; They will eat up your flocks and your herds; They will eat up your vines and your fig trees; They will demolish with the sword your fortified cities, In which you trust.
Verse_Ch: 5:18 耶和华说，甚至到那些日子，我也不将你们毁灭净尽。 ###EN### Yet even in those days, declares Jehovah, I will not make a full end of you.
Verse_Ch: 5:19 百姓若说，耶和华我们的神，为什么向我们行这一切事呢？你就对他们说，你们怎样离弃了我，在你们的地上事奉外邦神，也必照样在不属你们的地 上事奉外邦人。 ###EN### And when they say, Why has Jehovah our God done all these things to us? you shall say to them, As you have forsaken Me and served foreign gods in your land, so you will serve strangers in a land that is not yours.
Verse_Ch: 5:20 当将这话传扬在雅各家，报告在犹大家，说， ###EN### Declare this in the house of Jacob, And announce it in the house of Judah, saying,
Verse_Ch: 5:21 愚昧无知的百姓阿，你们有眼不看，有耳不听，现在当听这话： ###EN### Now hear this, O people, who are foolish and without understanding, Who have eyes but do not see, Who have ears but do not hear:
Verse_Ch: 5:22 耶和华说，你们怎么不惧怕我呢？你们在我面前还不战兢么？我以永远的定例，用沙为界限，使海不得越过。波浪虽然翻腾，却不能得胜；虽然匉訇， 却不能越过。 ###EN### Do you not fear Me, declares Jehovah; Do you not tremble at My presence; Who have set the sand as a boundary for the sea By an eternal statute, so it cannot pass over it? Although its waves toss, they cannot prevail; Although they roar, they cannot pass over it.
Verse_Ch: 5:23 但这百姓有顽梗叛逆的心；他们竟偏离我而去。 ###EN### But this people has a stubborn and rebellious heart; They have turned aside and have gone away.
Verse_Ch: 5:24 他们心里也不说，我们应当敬畏耶和华我们的神；祂按时赐雨，就是秋雨春雨，又为我们定收割的节令，永存不废。 ###EN### And they do not say in their heart, Let us now fear Jehovah our God, who gives us rain, Both the early rain and the late rain, in its season, Who preserves the appointed weeks of the harvest for us.
Verse_Ch: 5:25 你们的罪孽使这些事转离，你们的罪使你们不能得好处。 ###EN### Your iniquities have turned these things away, And your sins have withheld from you what is good.
Verse_Ch: 5:26 因为在我民中有恶人，他们好像捕鸟的人埋伏窥探；他们设立圈套捕捉人。 ###EN### For wicked men are found among My people; They lie in wait like fowlers crouching; They set a trap, They catch men.
Verse_Ch: 5:27 笼内怎样满了雀鸟，他们的房中也照样充满诡诈；所以他们得成为大，而且富足。 ###EN### Like a cage full of birds, So their houses are full of deceit; Therefore they have become great and rich.
Verse_Ch: 5:28 他们肥胖光润，又作恶过甚；他们不为人伸冤，就是不为孤儿伸冤，反倒自己亨通，也不为穷人辨屈。 ###EN### They are fat; they are sleek; Indeed they surpass in deeds of wickedness; They do not judge the cause, The cause of the orphan, but they prosper; And the right of the needy they do not judge.
Verse_Ch: 5:29 耶和华说，我岂不因这些事讨罪呢？我岂不报复这样的国呢？ ###EN### Shall I not punish because of these things? Declares Jehovah; And on a nation such as this Shall My soul not avenge itself?
Verse_Ch: 5:30 这地有可惊骇、恐怖的事， ###EN### An appalling and horrible thing Has happened in the land:
Verse_Ch: 5:31 就是申言者说假预言，祭司凭自己的权柄管理；我的百姓也喜爱这样。但到了结局，你们要怎样行呢？ ###EN### The prophets prophesy falsely, And the priests rule by their own authority; And My people love it this way. But what will you do at the end of it?
Chapter_Header: 6
Verse_Ch: 6:1 便雅悯人哪，你们要逃出耶路撒冷，在提哥亚吹角，在伯哈基琳立号旗；因为有灾祸与大毁坏，从北方向下张望。 ###EN### Seek refuge, O children of Benjamin, From the midst of Jerusalem; And blow the trumpet in Tekoa And raise up a signal on Beth-haccerem; For evil looks down from the north, And great destruction.
Verse_Ch: 6:2 那秀美娇嫩的锡安女子，我必剪除。 ###EN### The comely and delicate one, The daughter of Zion, I will cut off.
Verse_Ch: 6:3 牧人必带他们的羊群到她那里，在她周围支搭帐棚，各在自己所占之地牧养。 ###EN### Shepherds will come to her With their flocks; They will pitch tents against her all around; They will feed each one in his place.
Verse_Ch: 6:4 你们要准备攻击她；起来罢，我们可以趁中午上去。我们有祸了，日已渐斜，晚影拖长了。 ###EN### Prepare war against her; Rise up, and let us go up at noon. Woe to us, for the day has declined, For the shadows of evening are lengthening.
Verse_Ch: 6:5 起来罢，我们可以夜间上去，毁坏她的宫殿。 ###EN### Rise up, and let us go up at night And destroy her palaces.
Verse_Ch: 6:6 因为万军之耶和华如此说，你们要砍伐她的树木，筑垒攻打耶路撒冷。这就是那该受惩罚的城，其中尽是欺压。 ###EN### For thus says Jehovah of hosts, Cut down her trees and build up A mound against Jerusalem. This is the city to be punished; In her midst there is only oppression.
Verse_Ch: 6:7 水池怎样使水清新，这城也照样在恶上推陈出新；在其间常听见强暴毁灭的事，病患损伤也常在我面前。 ###EN### As a cistern keeps its waters fresh, So she has kept her wickedness fresh. Violence and destruction are heard in her; Sickness and wounds are always before Me.
Verse_Ch: 6:8 耶路撒冷阿，你当受警戒，免得我与你生疏，免得我使你荒凉，成为无人居住之地。 ###EN### Be admonished, O Jerusalem, Lest My desire for you depart, Lest I make you a desolation, An uninhabited land.
Verse_Ch: 6:9 万军之耶和华如此说，他们必掳尽以色列余剩的民，如同摘净葡萄一样；你要像摘葡萄的人伸手到枝子上，摘了又摘。 ###EN### Thus says Jehovah of hosts, They will thoroughly glean like a vine The remnant of Israel; Pass your hand again over the branches Like a grape gatherer.
Verse_Ch: 6:10 现在我可以向谁说话作见证，使他们听呢？他们的耳朵未受割礼，不能听见。耶和华的话，他们以为羞辱，不以为喜悦。 ###EN### To whom shall I speak and testify, That they may hear? Indeed, their ear is uncircumcised, And they are unable to listen. See, the word of Jehovah has become a reproach to them; They have no delight in it.
Verse_Ch: 6:11 因此我被耶和华的忿怒充满，难以含忍；我要倾倒在街中的孩童和聚集的少年人身上；连夫带妻，并年老的与日子满足的，都必被擒拿。 ###EN### Yet I am full of the wrath of Jehovah; I am weary of holding it in. Pour it out upon the children in the street And upon the assembly of the young men together; For even the husband with the wife will be taken; The old man, with the one who is full of days.
Verse_Ch: 6:12 他们的房屋、田地和妻子，都必转归别人；我要伸手攻击这地的居民；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### And their houses will be turned over to others, Fields and wives together; For I will stretch out My hand Over the inhabitants of the land, Declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 6:13 因为他们从最小的到至大的，人人都贪图不义之财；从申言者到祭司，个个都行事虚谎。 ###EN### For from the least of them to the greatest of them, Everyone is wresting unjust gain; And from the prophet to the priest, Everyone is dealing falsely.
Verse_Ch: 6:14 他们轻轻忽忽的医治我百姓的损伤，说，平安了，平安了；其实没有平安。 ###EN### And they have healed The brokenness of My people slightly, Saying, Peace, peace; Although there is no peace.
Verse_Ch: 6:15 他们行可憎的事，知道惭愧么？不然，他们毫不惭愧，也不知羞耻。因此，他们必在仆倒的人中仆倒；我向他们讨罪的时候，他们必至跌倒；这是耶 和华说的。 ###EN### Were they ashamed when they committed abomination? They were not at all ashamed; They did not even know to blush. Therefore they will fall with those who fall; At the time I punish them, they will stumble, Says Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 6:16 耶和华如此说，你们当站在路上察看，访问古远的路径，那一条是善路，便行在其上；你们魂里就必得安息。他们却说，我们不行在其上。 ###EN### Thus says Jehovah, Stand by the ways and see, And ask for the ancient paths; Ask where the good way is, and walk in it; And you will find rest for your souls. But they said, We will not walk in it.
Verse_Ch: 6:17 我设立守望的人照管你们，说，要听角声。他们却说，我们不听。 ###EN### So I set watchmen over you, saying, Listen to the sound of the trumpet. But they said, We will not listen.
Verse_Ch: 6:18 列国阿，因此你们当听；会众阿，要知道我必怎样待他们。 ###EN### Therefore hear, O nations, And understand, O assembly, What I will do to them.
Verse_Ch: 6:19 地阿，当听，我必使灾祸临到这百姓，那是他们意念所结的果子，因为他们未曾听从我的言语，也厌弃了我的律法。 ###EN### Listen, O earth; I am now bringing evil On this people, The fruit of their thoughts; Because they have not listened to My words, And they have also rejected My law.
Verse_Ch: 6:20 从示巴出的乳香，从远方出的甜甘蔗，奉来给我有何益呢？你们的燔祭不蒙悦纳，你们的平安祭我也不喜悦。 ###EN### For what purpose does frankincense come to Me from Sheba, And sweet cane from a distant land? Your burnt offerings are not acceptable, And your sacrifices are not pleasing to Me.
Verse_Ch: 6:21 所以耶和华如此说，我要将绊脚石放在这百姓前面，父亲和儿子要一同跌在其上；邻舍与朋友，也都要灭亡。 ###EN### Therefore thus says Jehovah, I am now laying before this people stumbling blocks, And fathers and sons together Will stumble against them; A neighbor and his friend will perish.
Verse_Ch: 6:22 耶和华如此说，看哪，有一民从北方之地而来，有一大国从地极被激动来到。 ###EN### Thus says Jehovah, See, a people is coming from the land of the north, And a great nation is stirring from the uttermost parts of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 6:23 他们拿弓和枪，性情残忍，毫无怜悯；他们的声音，像海浪匉訇；锡安的女子阿，他们都骑马摆队，如上战场的人来攻击你。 ###EN### They grasp bow and spear; They are cruel and have no mercy; Their voice roars like the sea; And they ride upon horses, Set in array as a man for battle Against you, O daughter of Zion.
Verse_Ch: 6:24 我们听见了这风声，手就发软；痛苦将我们抓住，疼痛仿佛临产的妇人。 ###EN### We have heard its report; Our hands are feeble; Distress has seized us, Pain like a woman in childbirth.
Verse_Ch: 6:25 你们不要往田野去，也不要行在路上；因仇敌有刀剑，四围有惊吓。 ###EN### Do not go out into the field, And do not walk on the road; For the enemy has a sword; Terror is on every side.
Verse_Ch: 6:26 我的百姓阿，应当腰束麻布，辊在灰中。你要悲伤如丧独生子，痛痛哭号；因为灭命的要忽然临到我们。 ###EN### O daughter of my people, gird yourself in sackcloth And roll in ashes; Mourn as for an only son, A most bitter wailing; For suddenly the destroyer Will come upon us.
Verse_Ch: 6:27 我已立你在我民中为试验的人，为保障，使你知道并试验他们所行的路。 ###EN### I have set you as a trier among My people, as a fortress, That you may know and try their way.
Verse_Ch: 6:28 他们都是极悖逆的，是往来谗谤人的；他们是铜是铁，都行事败坏。 ###EN### All of them are most rebellious, Going about as slanderers; They are brass and iron; All of them act corruptly.
Verse_Ch: 6:29 风箱烧毁；铅被火烧尽；尽管炼而又炼，终是徒然，因为恶劣的尚未除掉。 ###EN### The bellows are burned; The lead is consumed by the fire; The refining continues in vain, For the wicked are not removed.
Verse_Ch: 6:30 人必称他们为被弃的银渣，因为耶和华已经弃掉他们。 ###EN### Men will call them rejected silver, Because Jehovah has rejected them.
Chapter_Header: 7
Verse_Ch: 7:1 从耶和华有话临到耶利米，说， ###EN### The word that came to Jeremiah from Jehovah, saying,
Verse_Ch: 7:2 你当站在耶和华殿的门口，在那里宣告这话，说，你们进这些门敬拜耶和华的一切犹大人，当听耶和华的话。 ###EN### Stand in the gate of the house of Jehovah, and proclaim this word there and say, Hear the word of Jehovah, all Judah, who enter through these gates to worship Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 7:3 万军之耶和华以色列的神如此说，你们当改正所行所为，我就使你们仍然安居在这地方。 ###EN### Thus says Jehovah of hosts, the God of Israel, Amend your ways and your deeds, and I will cause you to dwell in this place.
Verse_Ch: 7:4 你们不要倚靠虚谎的话，说，这些建筑是耶和华的殿，是耶和华的殿，是耶和华的殿。 ###EN### Do not trust in the words of falsehood that say, The temple of Jehovah, the temple of Jehovah, these buildings are the temple of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 7:5 你们若实在改正所行所为，在人和邻舍中间诚然施行公理， ###EN### But if you truly amend your ways and your deeds, if you truly execute justice between a man and his neighbor,
Verse_Ch: 7:6 不欺压寄居的和孤儿寡妇，在这地方不流无辜人的血，也不随从别神陷害自己； ###EN### If you do not oppress the sojourner, the orphan, and the widow, and do not shed innocent blood in this place, nor go after other gods to your own ruin;
Verse_Ch: 7:7 我就使你们仍然安居在这地方，就是我从古时所赐给你们列祖的地，直到永远。 ###EN### Then I will cause you to dwell in this place, in the land which I gave to your fathers from eternity to eternity.
Verse_Ch: 7:8 你们倚靠虚谎无益的话。 ###EN### See, you are trusting in words of falsehood that do not benefit you.
Verse_Ch: 7:9 你们偷盗、杀害、奸淫、起假誓、向巴力烧香、并随从素不认识的别神； ###EN### Will you steal, murder, and commit adultery, and swear falsely, and burn incense to Baal and go after other gods which you have not known,
Verse_Ch: 7:10 然后来到这称为我名下的殿，站在我面前说，我们得自由了；你们以为这样就可以行那一切可憎的事么？ ###EN### Then come and stand before Me in this house, which is called by My name, and say, We are delivered!-that you may do all these abominations?
Verse_Ch: 7:11 这称为我名下的殿，在你们眼中成了贼窝么？我都看见了；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### Has this house which is called by My name become a den of robbers in your eyes? Yet I, even I, have seen it, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 7:12 你们且往示罗我的地方，就是我先前给我名居住的地方，察看我因我百姓以色列的罪恶，向那地所行的。 ###EN### But go now to My place which was in Shiloh, where I caused My name to dwell at first, and see what I did to it because of the wickedness of My people Israel.
Verse_Ch: 7:13 耶和华说，现在因你们行了这一切的事，我也从早起来说话，告诉你们，你们却不听从，呼唤你们，你们却不答应； ###EN### And now, because you have done all these works, declares Jehovah, and I spoke to you, rising up early and speaking, but you did not listen, and I called you, but you did not answer;
Verse_Ch: 7:14 所以我要对付这称为我名下，你们所倚靠的殿，与我所赐给你们和你们列祖的地方，像我从前对付示罗一样。 ###EN### Therefore I will do to the house that is called by My name, in which you trust, and to the place that I gave you and your fathers as I have done to Shiloh.
Verse_Ch: 7:15 我必将你们从我面前赶出，正如赶出你们的众弟兄，就是以法莲的一切后裔。 ###EN### And I will cast you out from before Me, as I cast out all your brothers, all the seed of Ephraim.
Verse_Ch: 7:16 至于你，不要为这百姓祈祷，不要为他们呼求祷告，也不要向我为他们代求；因我必不听你。 ###EN### And as for you, do not pray for this people, nor lift up a ringing cry or a prayer for them; and do not intercede with Me, for I will not hear you.
Verse_Ch: 7:17 他们在犹大城邑中和耶路撒冷街上所行的，你没有看见么？ ###EN### Do you not see what they are doing in the cities of Judah and in the streets of Jerusalem?
Verse_Ch: 7:18 孩子捡柴，父亲烧火，妇女抟面，作饼给天后，又向别神浇奠祭，惹我发怒。 ###EN### The children gather wood, and the fathers light the fire, and the women knead the dough, to make cakes for the queen of heaven and to pour out drink offerings to other gods to provoke Me to anger.
Verse_Ch: 7:19 耶和华说，他们岂是惹我发怒呢？不是自己惹祸，以致脸上惭愧么？ ###EN### Are they provoking Me to anger? declares Jehovah. Are they not provoking themselves, to the shaming of their own faces?
Verse_Ch: 7:20 所以主耶和华如此说，我的怒气和忿怒，必倾倒在这地方，在人和牲畜身上，并田野的树木和地里的出产上；必如火着起，不能熄灭。 ###EN### Therefore thus says the Lord Jehovah, My anger and My wrath will be poured out on this place, on man and on beast and on the trees of the field and on the fruit of the ground; and it will burn and not be quenched.
Verse_Ch: 7:21 万军之耶和华以色列的神如此说，你们将燔祭加在平安祭上，吃肉罢。 ###EN### Thus says Jehovah of hosts, the God of Israel, Add your burnt offerings to your sacrifices and eat the flesh.
Verse_Ch: 7:22 因为我将你们列祖从埃及地领出来的那日，燔祭和平安祭的事，我并没有题说，也没有吩咐他们。 ###EN### For I did not speak to your fathers or command them in the day that I brought them out of the land of Egypt concerning burnt offerings and sacrifices.
Verse_Ch: 7:23 我只吩咐他们这事，说，你们当听从我的话，我就作你们的神，你们也作我的子民；你们要行在我所吩咐的一切道路上，就可以得福。 ###EN### But this is what I commanded them, saying, Hear My voice, and I will be your God, and you will be My people; and walk in all the way which I command you, that it may go well with you.
Verse_Ch: 7:24 他们却不听从，不侧耳而听，竟随从自己的计谋和顽梗的恶心而行，向后不向前。 ###EN### But they did not listen or incline their ear, but walked in the counsels and the stubbornness of their evil hearts and went backward and not forward.
Verse_Ch: 7:25 自从你们列祖出埃及地的那日，直到今日，我差遣我的众仆人申言者，到你们那里去，每日从早起来差遣他们。 ###EN### From the day that your fathers came out from the land of Egypt unto this day I have sent to you all My servants the prophets, daily rising up early and sending them.
Verse_Ch: 7:26 你们却不听从，不侧耳而听，竟硬着颈项，行恶比你们列祖更甚。 ###EN### But they did not listen to Me or incline their ear, but stiffened their neck; they did more evil than their fathers.
Verse_Ch: 7:27 你要将这一切的话告诉他们，他们却不肯听从；呼唤他们，他们却不肯答应。 ###EN### So you shall speak to them all these words, but they will not listen to you; and you shall call to them, but they will not answer you.
Verse_Ch: 7:28 你要对他们说，这就是不听从耶和华他们神的话，不受管教的国民；真理已经丧失，从他们口中断绝了。 ###EN### And you shall say to them, This is the nation which did not listen to the voice of Jehovah their God and did not take correction; the truth has perished and is cut off from their mouth.
Verse_Ch: 7:29 耶路撒冷阿，要剪发抛弃，在光秃的高处举哀；因为耶和华丢掉并离弃了惹祂盛怒的世代。 ###EN### Cut off your hair and throw it away, And take up a lamentation on the bare heights; For Jehovah has rejected and forsaken The generation of His overflowing wrath.
Verse_Ch: 7:30 耶和华说，犹大人行了我眼中看为恶的事，将他们的可憎之物设立在称为我名下的殿中，污秽这殿。 ###EN### For the children of Judah have done that which is evil in My sight, declares Jehovah; they have set their detestable things in the house which is called by My name, to defile it.
Verse_Ch: 7:31 他们在欣嫩子谷建筑陀斐特的邱坛，好在火中焚烧自己的儿女；这并不是我所吩咐的，也不是我心所起的意。 ###EN### And they have built the high places of Topheth, which is in the valley of the son of Hinnom, to burn their sons and their daughters in the fire, something I did not command, nor did it come up in My heart.
Verse_Ch: 7:32 耶和华说，因此日子将到，这地方不再称为陀斐特或欣嫩子谷，反倒称为杀戮谷；因为他们要在陀斐特葬埋尸首，因无别处可葬。 ###EN### Therefore, days are coming, declares Jehovah, when it will no longer be called Topheth, or the valley of the son of Hinnom, but the valley of slaughter; for they will bury in Topheth because there will be no other place.
Verse_Ch: 7:33 并且这百姓的尸首，必给空中的飞鸟和地上的野兽作食物，并无人哄赶。 ###EN### And the corpses of this people will become food for the birds of the sky and for the beasts of the earth; and no one will frighten them away.
Verse_Ch: 7:34 我必使犹大城邑中和耶路撒冷街上，欢喜和快乐的声音，新郎和新妇的声音，都止息了；因为这地必成为荒场。 ###EN### And I will cause the voice of gladness and the voice of joy to cease, the voice of the bridegroom and the voice of the bride, from the cities of Judah and from the streets of Jerusalem; for the land will become a waste.
Chapter_Header: 8
Verse_Ch: 8:1 耶和华说，到那时人必将犹大王的骸骨、犹大首领的骸骨、祭司的骸骨、申言者的骸骨、并耶路撒冷居民的骸骨，都从坟墓中取出来， ###EN### At that time, declares Jehovah, they will bring out the bones of the kings of Judah and the bones of its princes and the bones of the priests and the bones of the prophets and the bones of the inhabitants of Jerusalem from their graves.
Verse_Ch: 8:2 抛散在日头、月亮、和天上众星之下，就是他们从前所喜爱、所事奉、所随从、所求问、所敬拜的；这些骸骨不再收殓葬埋；必在地面上成为粪土。 ###EN### And they will spread them out to the sun and to the moon and to all the host of heaven, which they have loved and which they have served and which they have gone after and which they have sought and which they have worshipped; and they will not be gathered up or buried; they will be like dung on the surface of the ground.
Verse_Ch: 8:3 并且这恶族所剩下一切的余民，在我所赶他们到的各处，宁可拣选死不拣选生，这是万军之耶和华说的。 ###EN### And death will be chosen rather than life by all the remnant that remains of this evil family, that remains in all the places where I have driven them, declares Jehovah of hosts.
Verse_Ch: 8:4 你要对他们说，耶和华如此说，人跌倒，不再起来么？人转去，不再转回么？ ###EN### And you shall say to them, Thus says Jehovah, Do men fall and not rise again? If one turns away, does he not return?
Verse_Ch: 8:5 这耶路撒冷的民，为何恒久背道呢？他们持定诡诈，不肯回头。 ###EN### Why has this people Jerusalem Turned away in perpetual apostasy? They hold fast to deceit; They refuse to turn back.
Verse_Ch: 8:6 我留心听且听见了，他们说不正直的话；无人懊悔自己的恶行，说，我作了什么呢？他们各人转奔己路，如马直闯战场。 ###EN### I have listened carefully and heard; They have not spoken rightly; There is no one who repents of his wickedness, Saying, What have I done? Everyone turns to his own course, Like a horse rushing headlong into battle.
Verse_Ch: 8:7 空中的鹳鸟，知道来去的定期；斑鸠、燕子和白鹤，也守候当来的时令；我的百姓，却不知道耶和华的律例。 ###EN### Even the stork in the sky Knows its appointed times, And the turtledove and the swallow and the crane Keep the time of their coming; But My people do not know The ordinance of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 8:8 你们怎么说，我们有智慧，耶和华的律法在我们这里？看哪，经学家的假笔舞弄虚假。 ###EN### How can you say, We are wise, And the law of Jehovah is with us? But look, the false pen of the scribes Has turned it into falsehood.
Verse_Ch: 8:9 智慧人惭愧、惊惶、被擒拿；看哪，他们弃掉耶和华的话，还有什么智慧呢？ ###EN### The wise men are put to shame; They are dismayed and are taken; See, they have rejected the word of Jehovah; And what wisdom do they have?
Verse_Ch: 8:10 所以我必将他们的妻子给别人，将他们的田地给别人为业；因为他们从最小的到至大的，人人都贪图不义之财；从申言者到祭司，个个都行事虚谎。 ###EN### Therefore I will give their wives to others, Their fields to those who will possess them; For from the small unto the great, Everyone is wresting unjust gain; From the prophet even to the priest, Everyone is dealing falsely.
Verse_Ch: 8:11 他们轻轻忽忽的医治我百姓的损伤，说，平安了，平安了；其实没有平安。 ###EN### And they have healed The brokenness of the daughter of My people slightly, Saying, Peace, peace, Although there is no peace.
Verse_Ch: 8:12 他们行可憎的事，知道惭愧么？不然，他们毫不惭愧，也不知羞耻。因此，他们必在仆倒的人中仆倒；我向他们讨罪的时候，他们必至跌倒；这是耶 和华说的。 ###EN### Were they ashamed when they committed abomination? They were not at all ashamed; They did not even know to blush. Therefore they will fall with those who fall; At the time of their punishment they will stumble, Says Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 8:13 耶和华说，我必将他们收取净尽；葡萄树上必没有葡萄，无花果树上必没有无花果，叶子也必枯干；我所赐给他们的，已离开他们过去。 ###EN### I will utterly take them away, Declares Jehovah; There are no grapes on the vine, And there are no figs on the fig tree; Even the leaves are withered; And what I gave them has passed away from them.
Verse_Ch: 8:14 我们为何坐着不动？你们当聚集，进入坚固城，在那里静默不言；因为耶和华我们的神，使我们静默不言，又将苦毒的水给我们喝，都因我们得罪了 耶和华。 ###EN### Why do we sit? Gather yourselves, And let us go up to the fortified cities And be silent there, Because Jehovah our God has silenced us And made us drink poisonous water, Because we have sinned against Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 8:15 我们指望平安，却得不着好处；指望得医治的时候，却受了惊惶。 ###EN### We hoped for peace, but no good came; For a time of healing, but there was terror.
Verse_Ch: 8:16 从但听见敌人的马喷鼻气；他们的壮马发嘶声，全地就都震动。他们来吞灭这地和其上所有的，吞灭这城和其中的居民。 ###EN### The snorting of their horses Is heard from Dan; At the sound of the neighing of their stallions The whole land quakes. And they come and devour the land and its fullness, The city and those who dwell in it.
Verse_Ch: 8:17 因为我必打发毒蛇到你们中间，是没有法术能制伏的；它们必咬你们；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### For I will send among you serpents, Adders, for which there is no enchantment; And they will bite you, Declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 8:18 我有忧愁，愿得安慰！我心在我里面发昏。 ###EN### Oh, that there were comforting to me in sorrow! My heart within me is faint.
Verse_Ch: 8:19 听阿，是我百姓的哀声，从极远之地而来，说，耶和华不在锡安么？锡安的王不在其中么？耶和华说，他们为什么以雕制的偶像，和外邦的偶像，惹 我发怒呢？ ###EN### It is the voice of the cry of the daughter of my people From a land very far away: Is Jehovah not in Zion? Is her King not in her? Why have they provoked Me to anger With their graven images and with strange idols?
Verse_Ch: 8:20 收割已过，夏日已完，我们还未得救。 ###EN### The harvest has passed, the summer has ended, And we are not saved.
Verse_Ch: 8:21 申言者说，因我百姓的损伤，我也受了损伤。我哀痛；惊恐将我抓住。 ###EN### For the brokenness of the daughter of my people I am broken. I mourn; horror has taken hold of me.
Verse_Ch: 8:22 在基列岂没有乳香么？在那里岂没有医生么？我百姓为何不得痊愈呢？ ###EN### Is there no balm in Gilead? Is there no physician there? Why then has the recovery of the daughter of my people Not occurred?
Chapter_Header: 9
Verse_Ch: 9:1 但愿我的头为众水，我的眼为泪的泉源，我好为我百姓中被杀的人，昼夜哭泣！ ###EN### Oh, that my head were waters, And my eye a fountain of tears, That I might weep day and night For the slain of the daughter of my people!
Verse_Ch: 9:2 惟愿我在旷野有行路人住宿之处，使我可以离开我的民出去，因他们都是行奸淫的，是行诡诈的会众。 ###EN### Oh, that I had a traveler's lodging place in the wilderness That I might leave my people and go away from them, For all of them are adulterers and an assembly of treacherous men.
Verse_Ch: 9:3 他们弯起舌头像弓一样；在这地得势的，是谎言而非真理；他们乃是恶上加恶，并不认识我；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### They bend their tongue like their bow; Falsehood, and not truth, Prevails in the land; For they proceed from evil to evil, And they do not know Me, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 9:4 你们各人当谨防邻舍，不可信靠弟兄；因为弟兄尽行抓夺，邻舍都往来谗谤人。 ###EN### Let each man be on guard against his neighbor And not confide in any brother; For every brother only supplants, And every neighbor goes about as a slanderer.
Verse_Ch: 9:5 他们各人欺哄邻舍，不说真话；他们教导舌头说谎，劳劳碌碌的作孽。 ###EN### And everyone deceives his neighbor And does not speak the truth; They teach their tongue to speak falsehood; They weary themselves committing iniquity.
Verse_Ch: 9:6 你的住处在诡诈之中；他们因行诡诈不肯认识我；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### Your dwelling is in the midst of deceit; Through deceit they refuse to know Me, Declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 9:7 所以万军之耶和华如此说，我要熬炼、试验他们；不然，我因我百姓的罪该怎样行呢？ ###EN### Therefore thus says Jehovah of hosts, Indeed, I will refine them and test them; For what else can I do because of the daughter of My people?
Verse_Ch: 9:8 他们的舌头是致命的箭，说话诡诈。人与邻舍口说和平话，心却谋害他。 ###EN### Their tongue is a deadly arrow; It speaks deceit. Each speaks peaceably to his neighbor with his mouth, But in his heart he lays an ambush for him.
Verse_Ch: 9:9 耶和华说，我岂不因这些事讨他们的罪么？我魂岂不报复这样的国么？ ###EN### Shall I not punish them for these things? Declares Jehovah; And on a nation such as this Shall My soul not avenge itself?
Verse_Ch: 9:10 我要为山岭哭泣举哀，为旷野的草场扬声哀号，因为都已烧尽，甚至无人经过，人也听不见牲畜鸣叫；空中的飞鸟和地上的野兽，都已逃去。 ###EN### For the mountains I will take up a weeping and wailing, And for the pastures of the wilderness, a lamentation; Because they have been burned up so that no one passes through, And the sound of cattle is not heard; Both the birds of the sky and the beasts Have fled and have gone.
Verse_Ch: 9:11 我必使耶路撒冷变为乱堆，为野狗的住处；也必使犹大的城邑变为荒场，无人居住。 ###EN### And I will make Jerusalem a heap of ruins, A habitation of jackals; And I will make the cities of Judah A desolation without inhabitant.
Verse_Ch: 9:12 谁是智慧人可以明白这事？耶和华的口向谁说过，使他可以述说？这地为何毁灭，烧尽如同旷野，甚至无人经过？ ###EN### Who is the wise man who can understand this, and he to whom the mouth of Jehovah has spoken, that he might declare it? Why is the land destitute, burned like the wilderness, so that no one passes through?
Verse_Ch: 9:13 耶和华说，因为这百姓离弃我在他们面前所设立的律法，没有听从我的话，也没有遵行我的律法； ###EN### And Jehovah said, Because they have forsaken My law, which I set before them, and have not listened to My voice or walked in My law,
Verse_Ch: 9:14 只随从自己顽梗的心而行，照他们列祖所教训的，随从众巴力； ###EN### But have walked after the stubbornness of their heart and after the Baals, as their fathers taught them;
Verse_Ch: 9:15 所以万军之耶和华以色列的神如此说，我必将茵蔯给这百姓吃，又将苦毒的水给他们喝。 ###EN### Therefore thus says Jehovah of hosts, the God of Israel, I will feed them, this people, with wormwood and give them poisonous water to drink.
Verse_Ch: 9:16 我要把他们分散在列国中，就是他们和他们列祖素不认识的列国；我也要打发刀剑追杀他们，直到将他们灭尽。 ###EN### And I will scatter them among the nations, whom neither they nor their fathers knew, and send the sword after them until I have consumed them.
Verse_Ch: 9:17 万军之耶和华如此说，你们应当思想，将唱哀歌的妇女召来，又打发人召灵巧的妇女来； ###EN### Thus says Jehovah of hosts, Consider, and call for the mourning women to come, And send for the skillful women to come;
Verse_Ch: 9:18 叫她们速速为我们举哀，使我们眼泪汪汪，使我们的眼皮涌出水来。 ###EN### Let them hasten and take up a wailing for us, That our eyes may shed tears And our eyelids may pour forth water.
Verse_Ch: 9:19 因为听见哀声出于锡安，说，我们是怎样的败落！我们大大的蒙羞！因为我们撇下了这地，因为人拆毁了我们的住处。 ###EN### For a voice of wailing Was heard from Zion: How we are ruined! We are utterly put to shame! For we have forsaken the land Because they have cast down our dwellings.
Verse_Ch: 9:20 妇女们哪，你们当听耶和华的话，你们的耳朵要领受祂口中的言语；又当教导你们的女儿哀哭，各人教导自己的邻舍唱哀歌。 ###EN### Therefore listen, O women, to the word of Jehovah, And let your ear receive the word of His mouth; And teach your daughters wailing, And let each teach her neighbor a lamentation.
Verse_Ch: 9:21 因为死亡已经上来，进了我们的窗户，入了我们的宫殿，要从街道上剪除孩童，从宽阔处剪除少年人。 ###EN### For death has come up through our windows; It has entered our palaces To cut off the children from the streets, The young men from the open squares.
Verse_Ch: 9:22 你当说，耶和华如此说，人的尸首必倒在田野像粪土，又像收割的人遗落的一把禾稼，无人收取。 ###EN### Speak: Thus declares Jehovah, And the corpses of men will fall Like dung on the surface of the field And like a sheaf after the reaper, And there will be no one to gather them.
Verse_Ch: 9:23 耶和华如此说，智慧人不要因他的智慧夸口，勇士不要因他的勇力夸口，财主不要因他的财物夸口； ###EN### Thus says Jehovah, Let not the wise man glory in his wisdom, And let not the mighty man glory in his might; Let not the rich man glory in his riches.
Verse_Ch: 9:24 夸口的却因他有聪明，认识我是耶和华，又知道我喜悦在地上施行慈爱、公理和公义，以此夸口；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### But let him who glories glory in this, That he has insight and knows Me, That I am Jehovah who exercises lovingkindness, Justice, and righteousness on earth; For in these things I delight, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 9:25 耶和华说，日子将到，我要惩罚一切受过割礼，心却没有受割礼的； ###EN### Indeed, days are coming, declares Jehovah, when I will punish all those who are circumcised and yet uncircumcised:
Verse_Ch: 9:26 我要惩罚埃及、犹大、以东、亚扪人、摩押、和一切住在旷野剃周围胡须的；因为列国人都没有受割礼，以色列全家心中也没有受割礼。 ###EN### Egypt and Judah and Edom and the children of Ammon and Moab and all those who cut the corners of their beards, who inhabit the wilderness; for all the nations are uncircumcised, and all the house of Israel is uncircumcised in heart.
Chapter_Header: 10
Verse_Ch: 10:1 以色列家阿，要听耶和华对你们所说的话。 ###EN### Hear the word which Jehovah speaks to you, O house of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 10:2 耶和华如此说，你们不要学列国的行径，也不要为天象惊惶，虽然列国为此事惊惶。 ###EN### Thus says Jehovah, Do not learn the way of the nations, And do not be terrified by the signs of the heavens, Although the nations are terrified by them.
Verse_Ch: 10:3 众民的风俗是虚空的，他们的神是从树林中砍下的树，是匠人用斧子作成的手工。 ###EN### For the customs of the peoples are vanity, Because their god is a tree cut from the forest, The work of the hands of a craftsman with an ax.
Verse_Ch: 10:4 他用金银妆饰，用钉子和锤子钉牢，使它不动摇。 ###EN### He adorns it with silver and with gold; They fasten it with nails and hammers So that it cannot totter.
Verse_Ch: 10:5 它们好像瓜田里的柱子，不能说话；它们不能行走，必须有人抬着。你们不要怕它们，因为它们不能降祸，也无力降福。 ###EN### They are like a post in a cucumber field, And they cannot speak; They must be carried Because they cannot walk. Do not be afraid of them, For they cannot do evil, And neither is it in them to do good.
Verse_Ch: 10:6 耶和华阿，没有像你的；你本为大，你的名大有能力。 ###EN### There is none like You, O Jehovah; You are great, And Your name is great in might.
Verse_Ch: 10:7 万国的王阿，谁不敬畏你？敬畏你本是合宜的，因为在列国的智慧人中，并万国之中，没有像你的。 ###EN### Who would not fear You, O King of the nations? For it befits You, For among all the wise of the nations And in all their kingdoms There is none like You.
Verse_Ch: 10:8 他们尽都是愚蠢、愚昧的；偶像的训诲算什么？它不过是木头。 ###EN### But they are altogether stupid and foolish; The instruction of their idols is mere wood.
Verse_Ch: 10:9 有银子打成片，是从他施带来的，并有从乌法来的金子，都是匠人的作品和金匠的手工；又有蓝色紫色料的衣服，都是巧匠的作品。 ###EN### Beaten silver Is brought from Tarshish, And gold from Uphaz, The work of a craftsman And of the hands of a goldsmith. Their clothing is blue and purple; All of them are the work of skillful men.
Verse_Ch: 10:10 惟耶和华是真神，是活神，是永远的王。祂一发怒，地就震动；祂一恼恨，列国都抵受不住。 ###EN### But Jehovah is the true God; He is the living God and the eternal King. At His wrath the earth quakes, And the nations cannot endure His indignation.
Verse_Ch: 10:11 你们要对他们如此说，那些不是造作天地的神，必从地上、从天下灭亡。 ###EN### Thus you shall say to them, The gods that did not make the heavens and the earth, these will perish from the earth and from under the heavens.
Verse_Ch: 10:12 耶和华用能力造作大地，用智慧建立世界，用聪明铺张诸天。 ###EN### It is He who made the earth by His power, Who established the world by His wisdom, And by His understanding He stretched out the heavens.
Verse_Ch: 10:13 祂一发声，空中便有多水激动；祂使云雾从地极上升；祂为雨造闪电，从祂府库中带出风来。 ###EN### When He utters His voice, there is a tumult of waters in the heavens, And He causes the vapors to rise from the ends of the earth; He makes lightning for the rain And brings forth wind from His treasuries.
Verse_Ch: 10:14 各人都愚蠢，毫无知识；各金匠都因自己雕制的偶像羞愧；他所铸的像是虚假的，其中并无气息。 ###EN### Every man is stupid, without knowledge; Every goldsmith is put to shame by his idol; For his molten image is falsehood, And there is no breath in them.
Verse_Ch: 10:15 这些都是虚无的，是迷惑人的作品；到讨罪的时候，必要灭亡。 ###EN### They are vanity, the work of delusion; At the time of their punishment they will perish.
Verse_Ch: 10:16 雅各的分不像这些；因祂是形成万有的，以色列也是祂产业的支派；万军之耶和华是祂的名。 ###EN### The Portion of Jacob is not like these; For He is the One who formed everything, And Israel is the tribe of His inheritance; Jehovah of hosts is His name.
Verse_Ch: 10:17 受围困的居民哪，从地上收拾你的包袱罢。 ###EN### Gather up your bundle from the ground, O inhabitant under siege.
Verse_Ch: 10:18 因为耶和华如此说，这时候我必将此地的居民甩出去，又必将困苦加在他们身上，使他们受困苦。 ###EN### For thus says Jehovah, I will sling out The inhabitants of the land At this time, And I will bring distress on them, That they may find it.
Verse_Ch: 10:19 民说，祸哉，我受损伤！我的创伤严重。我却说，这真是我的痛苦，我必须忍受。 ###EN### Woe is me because of my hurt! My wound is grievous. But I said, Truly this is my affliction, And I must bear it.
Verse_Ch: 10:20 我的帐棚毁坏，我的绳索都折断了。我的儿女离我出去，没有了。无人再支搭我的帐棚，挂起我的幔子。 ###EN### My tent is destroyed, and all my cords are broken; My children have gone from me and they are not; There is no one who will spread out my tent again And set up my curtains.
Verse_Ch: 10:21 因为牧人都是愚蠢，没有寻求耶和华；所以他们不得顺利，他们的羊群也都分散。 ###EN### For the shepherds are stupid And have not sought Jehovah; Therefore they have not prospered, And all their flock is scattered.
Verse_Ch: 10:22 有风声！敌人来了，有大扰乱从北方之地出来，要使犹大城邑变为荒凉，成为野狗的住处。 ###EN### The sound of a report! Here it comes, Even a great commotion from the land of the north, To make the cities of Judah A desolation, a habitation of jackals.
Verse_Ch: 10:23 耶和华阿，我晓得人的道路不由自己；行走的人，也不能定自己的脚步。 ###EN### I know, O Jehovah, That a man's way is not in himself; It is not in the man who walks To direct his step.
Verse_Ch: 10:24 耶和华阿，求你适度管教我；不要在你的怒中管教我，恐怕使我归于无有。 ###EN### Correct me, O Jehovah, but in measure, Not in Your anger lest You bring me to nothing.
Verse_Ch: 10:25 愿你将忿怒倾在不认识你的列国中，和不呼求你名的各族上；因为他们吞了雅各，不但吞了而且灭绝，把他的住处变为荒场。 ###EN### Pour out Your wrath on the nations Who do not know You And upon the families Who do not call upon Your name; For they have consumed Jacob, yes, consumed him and brought him to an end, And they have desolated his habitation.
Chapter_Header: 11
Verse_Ch: 11:1 从耶和华有话临到耶利米，说， ###EN### The word that came to Jeremiah from Jehovah, saying,
Verse_Ch: 11:2 当听这约的话，并将这些话告诉犹大人和耶路撒冷的居民。 ###EN### Listen to the words of this covenant and speak them to the men of Judah and to the inhabitants of Jerusalem.
Verse_Ch: 11:3 你要对他们说，耶和华以色列的神如此说，不听从这约之话的人，必受咒诅。 ###EN### And you shall say to them, Thus says Jehovah the God of Israel, Cursed is the man who does not listen to the words of this covenant,
Verse_Ch: 11:4 这约是我将你们列祖从埃及地领出来，脱离铁炉的那日所吩咐他们的，说，你们要听从我的话，照我所吩咐的一切去行；这样，你们就必作我的子民， 我也必作你们的神； ###EN### Which I commanded your fathers in the day that I brought them out of the land of Egypt, from the iron furnace, saying, Listen to My voice and do the things according to all which I command you; and you will be My people and I will be your God,
Verse_Ch: 11:5 我好坚定向你们列祖所起的誓，给他们流奶与蜜之地，正如今日一样。我就回答说，耶和华阿，阿们。 ###EN### That I may establish the oath which I swore to your fathers, to give them a land flowing with milk and honey, as it is this day. And I answered and said, Amen, Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 11:6 耶和华对我说，你要在犹大城邑中，和耶路撒冷街道上，宣告这一切话，说，你们当听从遵行这约的话。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to me, Proclaim all these words in the cities of Judah and in the streets of Jerusalem, saying, Hear the words of this covenant and do them.
Verse_Ch: 11:7 因为我将你们列祖从埃及地领上来的那日，曾郑重的警戒他们；直到今日，都是从早起来警戒他们，说，你们当听从我的话。 ###EN### For I solemnly warned your fathers in the day that I brought them up from the land of Egypt, even to this day, rising up early and warning, saying, Listen to My voice.
Verse_Ch: 11:8 他们却不听从，不侧耳而听，竟都按自己顽梗的恶心而行；所以我使这约中一切咒诅的话临到他们，这约是我吩咐他们行的，他们却不去行。 ###EN### But they did not listen or incline their ear, but all walked in the stubbornness of their evil heart; therefore I brought upon them all the words of this covenant, which I commanded them to do, and they have not done them.
Verse_Ch: 11:9 耶和华对我说，在犹大人和耶路撒冷居民中，有同谋背叛的事。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to me, A conspiracy has been found among the men of Judah and the inhabitants of Jerusalem.
Verse_Ch: 11:10 他们转回到他们先祖的罪孽中，不肯听我的话，又随从别神，事奉他们；以色列家和犹大家违背了我与他们列祖所立的约。 ###EN### They have turned back to the iniquities of their forefathers, who refused to listen to My words, and they have gone after other gods to serve them. The house of Israel and the house of Judah have broken My covenant which I made with their fathers.
Verse_Ch: 11:11 所以耶和华如此说，我必使灾祸临到他们，是他们不能逃脱的；他们必向我哀求，我却不听。 ###EN### Therefore thus says Jehovah, I am about to bring evil upon them, from which they cannot escape; and they will cry to Me, but I will not listen to them.
Verse_Ch: 11:12 那时犹大城邑的人，和耶路撒冷的居民，要去哀求他们烧香所供奉的神；只是他们遭难的时候，这些神毫不拯救他们。 ###EN### Then the cities of Judah and the inhabitants of Jerusalem will go and cry to the gods to whom they burn incense, but they will not save them at all in the time of their trouble.
Verse_Ch: 11:13 犹大阿，你神的数目与你城的数目相等；你为那可耻之物所立的坛，就是向巴力烧香的坛，与耶路撒冷街道的数目相等。 ###EN### For according to the number of your cities are your gods, O Judah, and according to the number of the streets of Jerusalem you have set up altars to that shameful thing, altars to burn incense to Baal.
Verse_Ch: 11:14 至于你，不要为这百姓祈祷，不要为他们呼求祷告；因为他们遭难向我呼求的时候，我必不听。 ###EN### And as for you, do not pray for this people, nor lift up a ringing cry or a prayer for them; for I will not hear when they call to Me because of their trouble.
Verse_Ch: 11:15 我所亲爱的既与许多人行淫，圣肉也离了你，你在我殿中作什么呢？你作恶就喜乐。 ###EN### What has My beloved to do in My house, Since she has committed lewdness with many And the holy flesh has passed from you? When you do evil, then you rejoice.
Verse_Ch: 11:16 耶和华曾给你起名叫青翠的橄榄树，外形华美，又结好果子；如今祂用哄嚷之声，点火在其上，枝子也烧毁了。 ###EN### Jehovah called your name, A flourishing olive tree, beautiful in fruit and form; With the sound of a great tumult He has set fire to it, And its branches are broken.
Verse_Ch: 11:17 原来栽培你的万军之耶和华已经说，要降祸攻击你，是因以色列家和犹大家行恶，向巴力烧香，惹我发怒，是自作自受。 ###EN### And Jehovah of hosts, who planted you, has pronounced evil against you because of the evil of the house of Israel and of the house of Judah, which they have done for themselves, to provoke Me to anger by burning incense to Baal.
Verse_Ch: 11:18 耶和华指示我，我就知道；你又将他们所行的，给我指明。 ###EN### And Jehovah made it known to me, so I knew; then You showed me their deeds.
Verse_Ch: 11:19 我像柔顺的羊羔被牵去宰杀，并不知道他们设计谋害我，说，我们把树连果子都毁灭罢，将他从活人之地剪除，使他的名不再被记念。 ###EN### And I was like a gentle lamb led to the slaughter, and I did not know that they devised devices against me, saying, Let us destroy the tree with its fruit, and let us cut him off from the land of the living that his name be remembered no longer.
Verse_Ch: 11:20 按公义判断，察验人肺腑心肠的万军之耶和华阿，愿我看见你在他们身上报仇，因我将我的案件向你禀明了。 ###EN### But, O Jehovah of hosts, who judges righteously, Who tests the inward parts and the heart, Let me see Your vengeance on them, For I have revealed my cause to You.
Verse_Ch: 11:21 所以耶和华论到寻索你命的亚拿突人如此说，他们说，你不要奉耶和华的名说预言，免得你死在我们手中； ###EN### Therefore thus says Jehovah concerning the men of Anathoth, who seek your life, saying, Do not prophesy in the name of Jehovah, that you may not die by our hand;
Verse_Ch: 11:22 所以万军之耶和华如此说，我必惩罚他们，他们的少年人必被刀剑杀死；他们的儿女必因饥荒死亡。 ###EN### Therefore thus says Jehovah of hosts, I am about to punish them: The young men will die by the sword; their sons and their daughters will die by famine;
Verse_Ch: 11:23 他们必没有余剩的人，因为在向他们讨罪之年，我必使灾祸临到亚拿突人。 ###EN### And they will have no remnant, because I will bring evil to the men of Anathoth in the year of their visitation.
Chapter_Header: 12
Verse_Ch: 12:1 耶和华阿，我与你争辩的时候，你显为公义；但我还要与你理论你的判决：恶人的道路为何亨通呢？大行诡诈的为何得安逸呢？ ###EN### You are righteous, O Jehovah, When I plead my cause with You; Yet I will speak with You of Your judgments: Why does the way of the wicked prosper? Why are all those who deal treacherously at ease?
Verse_Ch: 12:2 你栽种了他们，他们也扎根、长大、并结出果子。他们的口与你相近，他们的心肠却远离你。 ###EN### You have planted them; they have also taken root; They go on and bring forth fruit. You are near, in their mouth, But far from their inward parts.
Verse_Ch: 12:3 耶和华阿，你晓得我，看见我，察验我向你是怎样的心。求你将他们拉出来，好像将宰的羊，将他们分别出来，等候宰杀的日子。 ###EN### And You, O Jehovah, know me; You see me And try my heart toward You. Pull them out like sheep for the slaying, And set them apart for the day of slaughter.
Verse_Ch: 12:4 这地悲哀，遍野的青草枯干，要到几时呢？因其上居民的恶行，牲畜和飞鸟都灭绝了；他们曾说，祂看不见我们的结局。 ###EN### How long will the land mourn And the grass of every field dry up? Because of the wickedness of those who dwell in it, Beasts and birds are swept away, Because they said, He will not see our end.
Verse_Ch: 12:5 耶和华说，你若与步行的人同跑，尚且疲累，怎能与马赛跑呢？你在平安之地虽然安稳，在约但河边的丛林要怎样行呢？ ###EN### If you have run with footmen and they have wearied you, How then will you compete with horses? If you are secure in a land of peace, How then will you do in the majesty of the Jordan?
Verse_Ch: 12:6 因为连你弟兄和你父家，都用奸诈待你；他们也在你后边大声喊叫；虽向你说好话，你也不要信他们。 ###EN### For even your brothers and the house of your father, Even they have dealt treacherously with you; Even they have cried aloud after you. Do not believe them, although they speak good things to you.
Verse_Ch: 12:7 我离弃了我的殿宇，撇弃了我的产业，将我心里所亲爱的，交在她仇敌的手中。 ###EN### I have forsaken My house; I have abandoned My inheritance; I have given the beloved of My soul Into the hand of her enemies.
Verse_Ch: 12:8 我的产业向我如林中的狮子；她发声攻击我，因此我恨恶她。 ###EN### My inheritance has become to Me Like a lion in the forest; She lifted up her voice against Me, Therefore I hated her.
Verse_Ch: 12:9 我的产业，对于我岂是斑点的鸷鸟么？鸷鸟岂在她四围攻击她么？你们去聚集田野的百兽，带来吞吃罢。 ###EN### Is My inheritance a speckled bird of prey to Me? Are the birds of prey against her all around? Go, gather all the beasts of the field; Bring them to devour.
Verse_Ch: 12:10 许多牧人毁坏了我的葡萄园，践踏了我的分，使我美好的分变为荒凉的旷野。 ###EN### Many shepherds have destroyed My vineyard; They have trampled down My portion; They have made My pleasant portion A desolate wilderness.
Verse_Ch: 12:11 他们使地荒凉；地既荒凉，便向我悲哀；全地荒凉，因无人放在心上。 ###EN### They have made it a desolation; Desolate, it mourns to Me; The whole land has been desolated Because no one lays it to heart.
Verse_Ch: 12:12 灭命的来到旷野中一切光秃的高处，因为耶和华的刀，从地这边直到地那边，尽行杀灭；凡有血肉的，都不得平安。 ###EN### Upon all the bare heights in the wilderness Destroyers have come, For the sword of Jehovah devours From one end of the land to the other end of the land; No flesh has peace.
Verse_Ch: 12:13 他们种的是麦子，收的是荆棘；虽然耗尽了力气，却毫无益处；因耶和华的烈怒，你们必为自己的出产羞愧。 ###EN### They have sown wheat, and they reap thorns; They have worn themselves out, but they profit nothing; Therefore be ashamed of your produce Because of the burning anger of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 12:14 耶和华如此说，至于我的一切恶邻，就是侵犯我使百姓以色列所承受之产业的，我要将他们拔出本地，又要将犹大家从他们中间拔出来。 ###EN### Thus says Jehovah concerning all My evil neighbors, who have touched the inheritance which I caused My people Israel to inherit, I am about to pluck them up out of their land, and I will pluck up the house of Judah out from their midst.
Verse_Ch: 12:15 我拔出他们以后，必转过来怜恤他们，把他们再带回来，各归本业，各归本土。 ###EN### And after I have plucked them up, I will return and have compassion on them and bring them again, each one to his inheritance and each one to his land.
Verse_Ch: 12:16 他们若殷勤学习我百姓的道路，指着我的名起誓，说，我指着永活的耶和华起誓，正如他们从前教我百姓指着巴力起誓，他们就必建立在我百姓中 间。 ###EN### And if they will diligently learn the ways of My people, to swear by My name, saying, As Jehovah lives, even as they taught My people to swear by Baal, they will be built up in the midst of My people.
Verse_Ch: 12:17 他们若是不听，我必拔出那国，拔出而且毁灭；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### But if they do not listen, I will pluck up that nation, plucking it up and destroying it, declares Jehovah.
Chapter_Header: 13
Verse_Ch: 13:1 耶和华对我如此说，你去买一根麻布带子束腰，不可放在水中。 ###EN### Thus said Jehovah to me, Go and buy yourself a linen girdle, and put it on your loins, but do not put it in water.
Verse_Ch: 13:2 我就照着耶和华的话，买了一根带子束腰。 ###EN### So I bought a girdle according to the word of Jehovah and put it upon my loins.
Verse_Ch: 13:3 耶和华的话第二次临到我，说， ###EN### And the word of Jehovah came to me a second time, saying,
Verse_Ch: 13:4 要拿着你所买的腰带，就是你腰上的带子，起来往伯拉河去，将腰带藏在那里的磐石穴中。 ###EN### Take the girdle which you bought, which is upon your loins, and rise up; go to the Euphrates, and hide it there in a cleft of the rock.
Verse_Ch: 13:5 我就去，照着耶和华所吩咐我的，将腰带藏在伯拉河边。 ###EN### And I went and I hid it by the Euphrates, as Jehovah had commanded Me.
Verse_Ch: 13:6 过了多日，耶和华对我说，你起来，往伯拉河去，将我吩咐你藏在那里的腰带取出来。 ###EN### And at the end of many days Jehovah said to me, Rise up; go to the Euphrates, and take from there the girdle which I commanded you to hide there.
Verse_Ch: 13:7 我就往伯拉河去，在那里挖掘，将腰带从我所藏的地方取出来；见腰带已经变坏，毫无用处了。 ###EN### And I went to the Euphrates and dug, and I took the girdle from the place where I had hidden it; and there the girdle was, spoiled and good for nothing.
Verse_Ch: 13:8 耶和华的话临到我，说， ###EN### And the word of Jehovah came to me, saying,
Verse_Ch: 13:9 耶和华如此说，我必照样败坏犹大的骄傲，和耶路撒冷的大骄傲。 ###EN### Thus says Jehovah, Even so I will destroy the pride of Judah and the great pride of Jerusalem.
Verse_Ch: 13:10 这恶民不肯听我的话，按自己顽梗的心而行，随从别神，事奉敬拜它们，也必像这腰带，毫无用处。 ###EN### This evil people, who refuse to hear My words, who walk in the stubbornness of their heart and go after other gods to serve them and to worship them, will be even like this girdle, which is good for nothing.
Verse_Ch: 13:11 耶和华说，腰带怎样紧贴人腰，照样，我也使以色列全家和犹大全家紧贴我，好叫他们作我的子民，使我得名声，得赞美，得荣耀；他们却不肯听。 ###EN### For as this girdle clings to the loins of a man, so I have caused all the house of Israel and all the house of Judah to cling to Me, declares Jehovah, that they might be to Me a people and a name and a praise and a glory; but they would not listen.
Verse_Ch: 13:12 你要将这话对他们说，耶和华以色列的神如此说，各皮袋都要盛满酒。他们必对你说，我们岂不确知各皮袋都要盛满酒么？ ###EN### And you shall speak to them this word, Thus says Jehovah the God of Israel, Every wineskin will be filled with wine. And they will say to you, Do we not know very well that every wineskin will be filled with wine?
Verse_Ch: 13:13 你就要对他们说，耶和华如此说，我必使这地的一切居民，就是坐大卫宝座的君王，和祭司、申言者、并耶路撒冷的一切居民，都酩酊大醉。 ###EN### Then you shall say to them, Thus says Jehovah, I am about to fill all the inhabitants of this land and the kings who sit in David's place on his throne and the priests and the prophets and all the inhabitants of Jerusalem with drunkenness,
Verse_Ch: 13:14 耶和华说，我要使他们彼此相碰，就是父与子彼此相碰；我必不顾惜，不可怜，不怜恤，以致灭绝他们。 ###EN### And I will dash them one against the other, both the fathers and the sons together, declares Jehovah; I will not spare or pity or have compassion so as not to destroy them.
Verse_Ch: 13:15 你们当听，当侧耳而听，不要骄傲；因为耶和华已经说了。 ###EN### Hear and give ear and do not be proud, For Jehovah has spoken.
Verse_Ch: 13:16 耶和华你们的神未使黑暗来到，你们的脚未在昏暗山上绊跌之先，当将荣耀归给祂；你们盼望光，祂却使光变为死荫，成为幽暗。 ###EN### Give glory to Jehovah your God, Before He brings darkness, And before your feet stumble on the twilight mountains; And you will look for light, But He will turn it into a shadow of death And make it deep darkness.
Verse_Ch: 13:17 你们若不听这话，我必因你们的骄傲，在暗地哭泣；我眼必痛哭流泪，因为耶和华的群羊被掳去了。 ###EN### And if you will not hear it, My soul will weep in secret places for your pride; And my eye will weep bitterly and shed tears, Because the flock of Jehovah has been taken captive.
Verse_Ch: 13:18 你要对君王和太后说，你们当自卑坐下，因你们的华冠，已经从头上脱落了。 ###EN### Say to the king and to the queen mother, Humble yourselves and sit down, For your beautiful crown Has come down from your heads.
Verse_Ch: 13:19 南方的城尽都关闭，无人开放；全犹大都被迁走，全被迁走了。 ###EN### The cities of the south have been shut up, And there is no one to open them; All Judah has been taken into exile, Wholly taken into exile.
Verse_Ch: 13:20 你们要举目观看从北方来的人；先前赐给你的群羊，就是你佳美的群羊，如今在那里呢？ ###EN### Lift up your eyes, And see those who come from the north. Where is the flock that was given to you, Your beautiful sheep?
Verse_Ch: 13:21 耶和华立你自己所教导、作你朋友的，为首辖制你，那时你还有什么话说呢？痛苦岂不将你抓住，像产难的妇人么？ ###EN### What will you say when He appoints over you as head Those whom you yourself have trained to be your friends? Will not pains take hold of you, Like those of a woman in travail?
Verse_Ch: 13:22 你若心里说，这些事为何临到我？你的衣裙揭起，你的脚跟受伤，是因你的罪孽甚大。 ###EN### And if you say in your heart, Why have these things happened to me? It is because of the greatness of your iniquity that your skirts are uncovered, That your heels suffer violence.
Verse_Ch: 13:23 古实人岂能改变皮肤呢？豹岂能改变斑点呢？若能，你们这习惯行恶的，便能行善了。 ###EN### Can the Cushite change his skin, Or the leopard his spots? Then you also may be able to do good, Who are accustomed to do evil.
Verse_Ch: 13:24 所以我必使他们四散，像碎秸被旷野的风吹走一样。 ###EN### Therefore I will scatter them like chaff driven By the wind of the wilderness.
Verse_Ch: 13:25 耶和华说，这是你所当得的，是我量给你的分，因为你忘记了我，倚靠了虚假。 ###EN### This is your lot, The portion measured out to you from Me, Declares Jehovah, Because you have forgotten Me And have trusted in falsehood.
Verse_Ch: 13:26 所以我也要剥除你的衣裙，蒙在你脸上，显出你的羞耻。 ###EN### I will also strip your skirts off over your head, And your shame will be seen.
Verse_Ch: 13:27 你那些可憎恶的事，就是在田野、在山上行奸淫，发嘶声，放荡淫乱的事，我都看见了。耶路撒冷阿，你有祸了！你不肯洁净，还要到几时呢？ ###EN### Your adulteries and your neighings, The lewdness of your fornication Upon the hills, in the field, Your detestable things-I have seen. Woe to you, O Jerusalem! How long a time will you still not be clean?
Chapter_Header: 14
Verse_Ch: 14:1 耶和华论到干旱之灾的话，临到耶利米： ###EN### The word of Jehovah that came to Jeremiah concerning the drought:
Verse_Ch: 14:2 犹大悲哀，城门衰败；众人披着黑衣坐在地上悲哀，耶路撒冷的哀声上扬。 ###EN### Judah mourns, And her gates languish; In black they mourn on the ground, And the cry of Jerusalem goes up.
Verse_Ch: 14:3 他们的贵胄打发家僮打水；他们来到水池，见没有水，就拿着空器皿，蒙羞惭愧，抱头而回。 ###EN### And their nobles send their servants for water; They come to cisterns, And they find no water; They return with their vessels empty; They are ashamed and confounded And cover their heads.
Verse_Ch: 14:4 耕地的也蒙羞抱头；因为无雨降在地上，地就干裂。 ###EN### Because the ground is cracked, For there has been no rain on the earth, The farmers are ashamed; They cover their heads.
Verse_Ch: 14:5 田野的母鹿，生下小鹿就撇弃，因为无草。 ###EN### For even the hind in the field gives birth and abandons its young Because there is no grass.
Verse_Ch: 14:6 野驴站在光秃的高处，喘气好像野狗；因为无草，眼目失明。 ###EN### And the wild asses stand on the bare heights; They pant after the wind like jackals; Their eyes fail, For there is no herbage.
Verse_Ch: 14:7 耶和华阿，虽然我们的罪孽作见证告我们，还求你为你名的缘故行事；我们本是多次背道，得罪了你。 ###EN### Although our iniquities testify against us, O Jehovah, act for Your name's sake, For our apostasies have become many; We have sinned against You.
Verse_Ch: 14:8 以色列的盼望，在患难时作他救主的阿，你为何在这地像寄居的，又像行路的只转来住一宵呢？ ###EN### O Hope of Israel, Its Savior in a time of distress, Why should You be like a sojourner in the land, Like a traveler who turns aside to lodge for the night?
Verse_Ch: 14:9 你为何像受惊的人，像不能救人的勇士呢？耶和华阿，你仍在我们中间，我们是称为你名下的人；求你不要离开我们。 ###EN### Why should You be like an astonished man, Like a mighty man who is unable to save? Yet You are in our midst, O Jehovah, And we are called by Your name; Do not leave us.
Verse_Ch: 14:10 耶和华对这百姓如此说，这百姓喜爱飘流，不约束自己的脚步；所以耶和华不喜悦他们，现今要记念他们的罪孽，追讨他们的罪。 ###EN### Thus says Jehovah to this people, Even so they have loved to wander; they have not restrained their feet. Therefore Jehovah has no delight in them; now He will remember their iniquity and punish their sins.
Verse_Ch: 14:11 耶和华又对我说，不要为这百姓祷告求好处。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to me, Do not pray for the welfare of this people.
Verse_Ch: 14:12 他们禁食的时候，我不听他们的呼求；他们献上燔祭和素祭，我也不悦纳；我却要用刀剑、饥荒、瘟疫，灭绝他们。 ###EN### When they fast, I will not listen to their cry; when they offer up a burnt offering and a meal offering, I will not accept them; but by sword and by famine and by pestilence I will consume them.
Verse_Ch: 14:13 我就说，唉，主耶和华阿，那些申言者常对他们说，你们必不看见刀剑，也不会有饥荒；因为我耶和华要在这地方赐你们确实的平安。 ###EN### And I said, Ah, Lord Jehovah! Indeed, the prophets say to them, You will not see sword, nor will you have famine, for I will give you assured peace in this place.
Verse_Ch: 14:14 耶和华对我说，那些申言者托我的名说假预言；我并没有打发他们，没有吩咐他们，也没有对他们说话。他们向你们预言的，乃是虚假的异象、占 卜、和虚无的事，以及自己心中的诡诈。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to me, The prophets prophesy falsehood in My name; I did not send them or command them or speak to them. They are prophesying to you a false vision and divination and a worthless thing and the deceit of their own heart.
Verse_Ch: 14:15 所以耶和华如此说，论到托我名说预言的那些申言者，我并没有打发他们，他们还说这地不至有刀剑饥荒；其实那些申言者必被刀剑饥荒灭绝。 ###EN### Therefore thus says Jehovah concerning the prophets who prophesy in My name, although I did not send them, yet they say, A sword and famine will not be in this land: By sword and by famine those prophets will be consumed.
Verse_Ch: 14:16 听他们说预言的百姓，必因饥荒刀剑被抛在耶路撒冷的街道上，无人葬埋；他们连妻子带儿女，都是如此；我必将他们的恶，倒在他们身上。 ###EN### And the people to whom they prophesy will be cast out into the streets of Jerusalem because of the famine and the sword; and there will be no one to bury them-them, their wives, and their sons and their daughters-and I will pour out their own wickedness on them.
Verse_Ch: 14:17 你要将这话对他们说，愿我眼流泪，昼夜不息；因为我民的处女受了极大的损伤，受了严重的创伤。 ###EN### And you shall speak this word to them, Let my eyes run down with tears Night and day, and let them not cease; For the virgin daughter of my people is broken with great brokenness, A very grievous wound.
Verse_Ch: 14:18 我若出往田间，就见有被刀杀的；我若进入城内，就见有因饥荒患病的；因为连申言者带祭司都必飘泊到他们素不认识的地去。 ###EN### If I go forth into the field-Look, those slain by the sword; And if I come into the city-Look, those diseased with famine. For both the prophet and the priest Will go about in a land that they do not know.
Verse_Ch: 14:19 你全然弃绝犹大么？你厌恶锡安么？你为何击打我们，以致我们无法得医治呢？我们指望平安，却得不着好处；指望得医治的时候，却受了惊惶。 ###EN### Have You utterly rejected Judah? Or does Your soul loathe Zion? Why have You stricken us So that there is no healing for us? We looked for peace, but no good came; And for a time of healing, but there was terror.
Verse_Ch: 14:20 耶和华阿，我们承认自己的恶，和我们列祖的罪孽；因我们得罪了你。 ###EN### We acknowledge, O Jehovah, our wickedness, The iniquity of our fathers, for we have sinned against You.
