Verse_Ch: 42:13 倘若你们说，我们不要住在这地，以致不听从耶和华你们神的话， ###EN### But if you say, We will not remain in this land, so that you do not listen to the voice of Jehovah your God,
Verse_Ch: 42:14 说，不，我们要进入埃及地，在那里我们看不见争战，听不见角声，也不至饥饿无食；我们必住在那里； ###EN### Saying, No, but we will go to the land of Egypt, where we will not see war or hear the sound of the trumpet or be hungry for bread, and we will dwell there;
Verse_Ch: 42:15 你们犹大余剩的人哪，现在要听耶和华的话：万军之耶和华以色列的神如此说，你们若定意要往埃及去，在那里寄居； ###EN### Then hear now the word of Jehovah, O remnant of Judah: Thus says Jehovah of hosts, the God of Israel, If indeed you set your faces to go to Egypt and go to sojourn there,
Verse_Ch: 42:16 你们所惧怕的刀剑，必在埃及地追上你们；你们所惧怕的饥荒，必在埃及紧紧的跟随你们；你们必死在那里。 ###EN### Then the sword, which you fear, will overtake you there in the land of Egypt, and the famine, about which you are worried, will follow hard after you there in Egypt; and you will die there.
Verse_Ch: 42:17 凡定意要进入埃及在那里寄居的，必遭刀剑、饥荒、瘟疫而死；他们必无一人存留，无人逃脱我所降与他们的灾祸。 ###EN### And all the men who set their faces to go to Egypt, to sojourn there, will die by sword, by famine, and by pestilence; and they will have no survivors or any who have escaped from the evil which I will bring on them.
Verse_Ch: 42:18 万军之耶和华以色列的神如此说，我怎样将我的怒气和忿怒倾在耶路撒冷的居民身上，你们进入埃及的时候，我也必照样将我的忿怒倾在你们身上。 你们必成为辱骂、惊骇、咒诅、羞辱，你们不得再见这地方。 ###EN### For thus says Jehovah of hosts, the God of Israel, As My anger and My wrath have been poured out on the inhabitants of Jerusalem, so My wrath will be poured out on you when you go to Egypt. And you will become an execration and an astonishment and a curse and a reproach, and you will see this place no more.
Verse_Ch: 42:19 犹大余剩的人哪，耶和华论到你们说，不要进入埃及去！你们要确实的知道，我今日作证警告你们了。 ###EN### Jehovah has spoken concerning you, O remnant of Judah, Do not go to Egypt! Know assuredly that today I have testified against you,
Verse_Ch: 42:20 你们是自欺了；因为你们差我到耶和华你们的神那里，说，求你为我们祷告耶和华我们的神，照耶和华我们神一切所说的告诉我们，我们就必遵行。 ###EN### That you deceived yourselves when you sent me to Jehovah your God, saying, Pray for us to Jehovah our God, and whatever Jehovah our God says, tell this to us, and we will do it.
Verse_Ch: 42:21 我今日告诉你们了，但耶和华你们的神为你们的事，差遣我到你们这里说的，你们一样也没有听从。 ###EN### And today I have told you, but you have not listened to the voice of Jehovah your God in anything for which He has sent me to you.
Verse_Ch: 42:22 现在你们要确实的知道，你们在所要去寄居之地，必遭刀剑、饥荒、瘟疫而死。 ###EN### And now therefore know assuredly that you will die by sword, by famine, and by pestilence in the place where you desire to go and sojourn.
Chapter_Header: 43
Verse_Ch: 43:1 耶利米向众百姓说完了耶和华他们神的一切话，就是耶和华他们神差遣他去对他们所说的一切话， ###EN### And when Jeremiah finished speaking to all the people all the words of Jehovah their God, with which Jehovah their God had sent him to them, all these words,
Verse_Ch: 43:2 何沙雅的儿子亚撒利雅，和加利亚的儿子约哈难，并一切狂傲的人，对耶利米说，你说谎言；耶和华我们的神并没有差遣你来说，你们不可进入埃及， 在那里寄居。 ###EN### Azariah the son of Hoshaiah and Johanan the son of Kareah and all the proud men spoke to Jeremiah, saying, You are speaking falsehood; Jehovah our God has not sent you to say, You shall not go to Egypt to sojourn there.
Verse_Ch: 43:3 这是尼利亚的儿子巴录挑唆你害我们，要将我们交在迦勒底人的手中，使他们杀死我们，或将我们迁徙到巴比伦去。 ###EN### But Baruch the son of Neriah is inciting you against us so as to give us into the hand of the Chaldeans that they may put us to death or take us into exile to Babylon.
Verse_Ch: 43:4 于是加利亚的儿子约哈难和一切军长，并众百姓，不听从耶和华的话住在犹大地。 ###EN### So Johanan the son of Kareah and all the captains of the forces and all the people did not listen to the voice of Jehovah to remain in the land of Judah.
Verse_Ch: 43:5 加利亚的儿子约哈难和一切军长，却将所余剩的犹大人，就是从被赶到的各国回来，要在犹大地寄居的人， ###EN### But Johanan the son of Kareah and all the captains of the forces took all the remnant of Judah, who had returned from all the nations where they had been driven in order to sojourn in the land of Judah,
Verse_Ch: 43:6 男人、妇女、孩童、和众公主，并护卫长尼布撒拉旦所留在沙番的孙子，亚希甘的儿子基大利那里的众人，与申言者耶利米，以及尼利亚的儿子巴录， 都带走了； ###EN### The men and the women and the little children and the king's daughters and every person whom Nebuzaradan the captain of the bodyguard had left with Gedaliah the son of Ahikam, the son of Shaphan, as well as Jeremiah the prophet and Baruch the son of Neriah;
Verse_Ch: 43:7 他们进入埃及地，(因他们不听从耶和华的话，)到了答比匿。 ###EN### And they came to the land of Egypt (for they did not listen to the voice of Jehovah) and came as far as Tahpanhes.
Verse_Ch: 43:8 在答比匿耶和华的话临到耶利米，说， ###EN### Then the word of Jehovah came to Jeremiah in Tahpanhes, saying,
Verse_Ch: 43:9 你在犹大人眼前要用手拿几块大石头，藏在砌砖的灰泥中，就是在答比匿法老的宫门那里； ###EN### Take large stones in your hand, and hide them in the mortar in the brickwork which is at the entrance of Pharaoh's house in Tahpanhes in the sight of the Jews.
Verse_Ch: 43:10 对他们说，万军之耶和华以色列的神如此说，我必打发并领来我的仆人巴比伦王尼布甲尼撒；在所藏的这些石头上，我要安置他的宝座；他必将华 盖支搭在其上。 ###EN### And say to them, Thus says Jehovah of hosts, the God of Israel, I am going to send and take Nebuchadrezzar the king of Babylon, My servant, and I will set his throne above these stones which I have hidden; and he will spread his canopy over them.
Verse_Ch: 43:11 他要来攻击埃及地：定为死亡的必至死亡，定为掳掠的必被掳掠，定为刀杀的必交刀杀。 ###EN### And he will come and strike the land of Egypt: those who are for death to death, and those who are for captivity to captivity, and those who are for the sword to the sword.
Verse_Ch: 43:12 我要在埃及诸神的庙中使火着起；巴比伦王要将庙宇焚烧，把他们掳去；他要披上埃及地，好像牧人披上外衣，从那里安然出去。 ###EN### And I will kindle a fire in the houses of the gods of Egypt, and he will burn them and carry them away captive; and he will wrap himself with the land of Egypt, as a shepherd wraps himself with his garment; and he will go out from there in peace.
Verse_Ch: 43:13 他必打碎埃及地伯示麦的柱像；用火焚烧埃及诸神的庙宇。 ###EN### And he will smash the pillars of Beth- shemesh, which is in the land of Egypt, and he will burn the houses of the gods of Egypt with fire.
Chapter_Header: 44
Verse_Ch: 44:1 有临到耶利米的话，论及一切住在埃及地的犹大人，就是住在密夺、答比匿、挪弗、巴忒罗地的犹大人，说， ###EN### The word that came to Jeremiah concerning all the Jews who dwelt in the land of Egypt, who dwelt at Migdol and at Tahpanhes and at Memphis and in the land of Pathros, saying,
Verse_Ch: 44:2 万军之耶和华以色列的神如此说，我所降与耶路撒冷和犹大各城的一切灾祸，你们都看见了；看哪，那些城邑今日荒凉，无人居住， ###EN### Thus says Jehovah of hosts, the God of Israel, You have seen all the evil that I have brought upon Jerusalem and upon all the cities of Judah; and see, today they are a desolation, and no one dwells in them,
Verse_Ch: 44:3 这是因他们所行的恶惹我发怒，去烧香事奉别神，就是他们和你们，并你们列祖所不认识的神。 ###EN### Because of their wickedness which they did to provoke Me to anger, in that they went to burn incense to serve other gods, which they did not know, neither they, you, nor your fathers.
Verse_Ch: 44:4 我从早起来差遣我的仆人众申言者到你们那里去，说，你们切不要行我所恨恶这可憎之事。 ###EN### Yet I sent to you all My servants the prophets, rising up early and sending them, saying, Do not do this abominable thing which I hate.
Verse_Ch: 44:5 他们却不听从，不侧耳而听，不转离恶事，仍向别神烧香。 ###EN### But they did not listen or incline their ear to turn from their wickedness, so as not to burn incense to other gods.
Verse_Ch: 44:6 因此，我的忿怒和怒气都倒出来，在犹大的城邑中和耶路撒冷的街道上，如火着起，以致成为荒废凄凉，正如今日一样。 ###EN### And My wrath and My anger poured forth and burned in the cities of Judah and in the streets of Jerusalem, and they became a waste and a desolation, as they are this day.
Verse_Ch: 44:7 现在耶和华万军之神，以色列的神如此说，你们为何作这大恶自害己命，使你们的男人、妇女、婴孩、和吃奶的，都从犹大中剪除，不留剩一人呢？ ###EN### And now thus says Jehovah the God of hosts, the God of Israel, Why do you do a great evil against your souls, so as to cut off from yourselves man and woman, little one and nursing child, from the midst of Judah, leaving yourselves no remnant,
Verse_Ch: 44:8 就是因你们手所作的，在所去寄居的埃及地，向别神烧香惹我发怒，使你们被剪除，在地上万国中令人咒诅、羞辱。 ###EN### Provoking Me to anger with the works of your hands, burning incense to other gods in the land of Egypt, where you have come to sojourn, so that you might be cut off and that you might become a curse and a reproach among all the nations of the earth?
Verse_Ch: 44:9 你们列祖的恶，犹大列王和他们后妃的恶，你们自己和你们妻子的恶，就是在犹大地、耶路撒冷街上所行的，你们都忘了么？ ###EN### Have you forgotten the wickedness of your fathers and the wickedness of the kings of Judah and the wickedness of their wives and your own wickedness and the wickedness of your wives, which they did in the land of Judah and in the streets of Jerusalem?
Verse_Ch: 44:10 你们到如今还没有痛悔，没有惧怕，没有遵行我在你们和你们列祖面前所设立的律法和条例。 ###EN### They have not become contrite even to this day, nor have they feared or walked in My law or in My statutes, which I set before you and before your fathers.
Verse_Ch: 44:11 所以万军之耶和华以色列的神如此说，我必向你们变脸降灾，以致剪除犹大众人。 ###EN### Therefore thus says Jehovah of hosts, the God of Israel, I will set My face against you for evil, even to cut off all Judah.
Verse_Ch: 44:12 那定意进入埃及地在那里寄居的，就是余剩的犹大人，我必把他们除去；他们必尽都灭绝，必在埃及地仆倒，必因刀剑、饥荒灭绝；从最小的到至 大的，都必遭刀剑、饥荒而死；他们必成为辱骂、惊骇、咒诅、羞辱。 ###EN### And I will take the remnant of Judah who have set their faces to go to the land of Egypt to sojourn there, and they will all be consumed; in the land of Egypt they will fall; by sword and by famine they will be consumed. From the small even unto the great, by sword and by famine they will die; and they will become an execration, an astonishment, and a curse and a reproach.
Verse_Ch: 44:13 我怎样用刀剑、饥荒、瘟疫惩罚耶路撒冷，也必照样惩罚那些住在埃及地的犹大人。 ###EN### And I will punish those who dwell in the land of Egypt, as I have punished Jerusalem: with sword, with famine, and with pestilence.
Verse_Ch: 44:14 甚至那些进入埃及地在那里寄居的，就是余剩的犹大人，没有一人能逃脱、幸存，而能归回犹大地，就是他们渴想归回居住之地；除了一些逃脱的 以外，他们都不能归回。 ###EN### And there will not be one who has escaped nor a survivor of the remnant of Judah, who went to sojourn there in the land of Egypt, even to return to the land of Judah, where they desire to return to dwell; for they will not return, except for some who will escape.
Verse_Ch: 44:15 那些住在埃及地巴忒罗，知道自己妻子向别神烧香的众民，与旁边站立的众妇女聚集成大群，回答耶利米，说， ###EN### Then all the men who knew that their wives burned incense to other gods and all the women who stood by, a great assemblage, even all the people who dwelt in Pathros in the land of Egypt, answered Jeremiah, saying,
Verse_Ch: 44:16 论到你奉耶和华的名向我们所说的话，我们必不听从。 ###EN### As for the word which you have spoken to us in the name of Jehovah, we will not listen to you.
Verse_Ch: 44:17 我们定要成就我们口中所出的一切话，向天后烧香、浇奠祭，按我们与我们列祖、君王、首领，在犹大的城邑中和耶路撒冷的街道上，素常所行的 一样；因为那时我们吃饱饭，享福乐，并不见灾祸。 ###EN### But we will surely do everything which has gone out of our mouth, burning incense to the queen of heaven and pouring out libations to her, just as we ourselves and our fathers, our kings, and our princes did in the cities of Judah and in the streets of Jerusalem; for we had plenty of food and were well off and did not see evil.
Verse_Ch: 44:18 自从我们停止向天后烧香、浇奠祭，我们倒缺乏一切，又因刀剑、饥荒灭绝。 ###EN### But since we ceased burning incense to the queen of heaven and pouring out libations to her, we have lacked everything and have been consumed by sword and by famine.
Verse_Ch: 44:19 妇女说，我们向天后烧香、浇奠祭，作饼给她，向她浇奠祭，难道没有我们的丈夫同着么？ ###EN### And when we burned incense to the queen of heaven and poured out libations to her, did we make cakes to her, making images of her and pouring out libations to her, without our husbands?
Verse_Ch: 44:20 耶利米对众民，论到一切那样回答他的男女众人，说， ###EN### Then Jeremiah spoke to all the people concerning the men and concerning the women, even concerning all the peo- ple who had given him that answer, saying,
Verse_Ch: 44:21 你们与你们列祖、君王、首领、并这地的百姓，在犹大城邑中和耶路撒冷街道上所烧的香，耶和华岂不记得，心中岂不思想么？ ###EN### As for the incense which you burned in the cities of Judah and in the streets of Jerusalem, you and your fathers, your kings and your princes, and the people of the land, did not Jehovah remember them, and did it not come up in His heart?
Verse_Ch: 44:22 耶和华因你们所作的恶，所行可憎的事，不能再容忍；所以你们的地成为荒凉、惊骇、咒诅，无人居住，正如今日一样。 ###EN### And Jehovah was no longer able to bear it because of the evil of your deeds, because of the abominations which you committed; therefore your land has become a desolation and an astonishment and a curse, without inhabitant, as it is this day.
Verse_Ch: 44:23 你们烧香，得罪耶和华，没有听从耶和华的话，没有遵行祂的律法、条例、法度；所以你们遭遇这灾祸，正如今日一样。 ###EN### Because you burned incense and because you sinned against Jehovah and did not listen to the voice of Jehovah or walk in His law or in His statutes or in His testimonies, therefore this evil has happened to you, as it is this day.
Verse_Ch: 44:24 耶利米又对众民和众妇女说，你们在埃及地的一切犹大人，当听耶和华的话： ###EN### Then Jeremiah said to all the people and to all the women, Hear the word of Jehovah, all Judah who are in the land of Egypt:
Verse_Ch: 44:25 万军之耶和华以色列的神如此说，你们和你们的妻子，都口中说，手里作，说，我们定要履行所许的愿，向天后烧香、浇奠祭；现在你们只管坚立 所许的愿，履行所许的愿罢。 ###EN### Thus speaks Jehovah of hosts, the God of Israel, saying, You and your wives have both spoken with your mouths and have fulfilled it with your hands, saying, We will surely perform our vows by which we have vowed to burn incense to the queen of heaven and to pour out libations to her. Establish then your vows, and by all means perform your vows.
Verse_Ch: 44:26 所以你们住在埃及地的一切犹大人，当听耶和华的话；耶和华说，我指着我的大名起誓，在埃及全地，我的名不再被任何一个犹大人的口称呼，说， 我指着主永活的耶和华起誓。 ###EN### Therefore hear the word of Jehovah, all Judah who dwell in the land of Egypt, I have sworn by My great name, says Jehovah: My name shall no longer be called upon by the mouth of any man of Judah in all the land of Egypt, saying, As the Lord Jehovah lives.
Verse_Ch: 44:27 我必向他们留意降祸不降福，在埃及地的一切犹大人必因刀剑、饥荒灭亡，直到灭尽。 ###EN### I will be watchful over them for evil and not for good, and all the men of Judah who are in the land of Egypt shall be consumed by sword and by famine until there is an end of them.
Verse_Ch: 44:28 逃脱刀剑，从埃及地归回犹大地的人数很少；一切余剩的犹大人，就是那些进入埃及地要在那里寄居的，必知道是谁的话立得住，是我的话呢？还 是他们的话？ ###EN### And those who escape the sword will return from the land of Egypt to the land of Judah few in number, and all the remnant of Judah who came to the land of Egypt to sojourn there will know whose word will be established, Mine or theirs.
Verse_Ch: 44:29 耶和华说，我在这地方惩罚你们，这是给你们的豫兆，使你们知道我降祸与你们的话，必要立得住。 ###EN### And this will be a sign to you, declares Jehovah, that I will punish you in this place, so that you will know that My words will surely be established against you for evil:
Verse_Ch: 44:30 耶和华如此说，我必将埃及王法老合弗拉交在他仇敌和寻索其命的人手中，像我将犹大王西底家交在他仇敌和寻索其命的巴比伦王尼布甲尼撒手中 一样。 ###EN### Thus says Jehovah, I will give Pharaoh Hophra, the king of Egypt, into the hand of his enemies, into the hand of those who seek his life, just as I gave Zedekiah the king of Judah into the hand of Nebuchadrezzar the king of Babylon, who was his enemy and sought his life.
Chapter_Header: 45
Verse_Ch: 45:1 申言者耶利米对巴录所说的话，是在犹大王约西亚的儿子约雅敬第四年，由尼利亚的儿子巴录将耶利米口中所说以下这些话写在书上，说， ###EN### The word which Jeremiah the prophet spoke to Baruch the son of Neriah, when he had written these words in a book from the mouth of Jeremiah, in the fourth year of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah, the king of Judah, saying,
Verse_Ch: 45:2 巴录阿，论到你，耶和华以色列的神如此说， ###EN### Thus says Jehovah the God of Israel, concerning you, O Baruch:
Verse_Ch: 45:3 你曾说，我有祸了！耶和华将忧愁加在我的痛苦上；我因唉哼而困乏，不得安歇。 ###EN### You said, Woe is me! For Jehovah has added sorrow to my pain; I am weary with my groaning and have not found rest.
Verse_Ch: 45:4 你要这样告诉他，耶和华如此说，我要拆毁我所建造的；我要拔出我所栽植的，在这全地我都要如此行。 ###EN### Thus you shall say to him, Thus says Jehovah, What I have built I am about to tear down; and what I have planted I am about to pluck up, even this whole land.
Verse_Ch: 45:5 你为自己图谋大事么？不要图谋，因我必使灾祸临到凡有血肉的；但你无论往那里去，我必将你的性命赐给你为掠物；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### And are you seeking great things for yourself? Do not seek them; for I am about to bring evil upon all flesh, declares Jehovah, but I will give your own life to you as spoil in all places where you may go.
Chapter_Header: 46
Verse_Ch: 46:1 耶和华论列国的话临到申言者耶利米。 ###EN### The word of Jehovah that came to Jeremiah the prophet concerning the nations:
Verse_Ch: 46:2 论埃及：关于埃及王法老尼哥的军队；这军队在伯拉河边的迦基米施，是巴比伦王尼布甲尼撒在犹大王约西亚的儿子约雅敬第四年所打败的。 ###EN### Concerning Egypt: Concerning the army of Pharaoh Neco, the king of Egypt, which was by the river Euphrates at Carchemish, which Nebuchadrezzar the king of Babylon struck down in the fourth year of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah, the king of Judah:
Verse_Ch: 46:3 你们要预备大小盾牌，往前上阵。 ###EN### Prepare the buckler and shield, And draw near to battle.
Verse_Ch: 46:4 你们要套上车，骑上马，顶盔站立，磨枪披甲。 ###EN### Harness the horses, And mount the steeds; And take your stand with helmets on; Polish the spears; Put on the armor.
Verse_Ch: 46:5 我为何看见他们惊惶，转身退后呢？他们的勇士被击溃了，急忙逃跑，并不回头；四围都是惊吓；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### Why have I seen it? They are dismayed; They are turning backward; And their mighty men are crushed and flee in hasty flight, And they do not look back; terror is on every side, Declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 46:6 不要让快跑的逃走，不要让勇士逃脱；他们在北方伯拉河边绊跌仆倒。 ###EN### Let not the swift one flee away And the mighty man escape; In the north by the river Euphrates They have stumbled and fallen.
Verse_Ch: 46:7 那像尼罗河涨发，像江河之水翻腾的是谁呢？ ###EN### Who is this who rises up like the Nile, Like rivers whose waters surge?
Verse_Ch: 46:8 埃及像尼罗河涨发，像江河的水翻腾。他说，我要涨发淹没这地；我要毁灭城邑，和其中的居民。 ###EN### Egypt rises up like the Nile, Even like rivers whose waters surge. And he says, I will rise up and will cover the land; I will destroy the city and the inhabitants in it.
Verse_Ch: 46:9 马匹阿，上去罢；战车阿，急行罢；勇士，就是手拿盾牌的古实人和弗人，并拉弓的路德族，都出去罢。 ###EN### Go up, O horses, And drive furiously, O chariots; And let the mighty men go forth: Cush and Put, who handle the shield, And the Ludim, who handle and bend the bow.
Verse_Ch: 46:10 这日是属主万军之耶和华的，是报仇的日子，要向敌人报仇；刀剑必吞吃得饱，饮血饮足；因为在北方之地伯拉河边，有献给主万军之耶和华的祭。 ###EN### For this day belongs to the Lord Jehovah of hosts, A day of vengeance to avenge Himself on His adversaries; And the sword will devour and be satisfied, And it will drink its fill of their blood; For there is a sacrifice to the Lord Jehovah of hosts In the land of the north by the river Euphrates.
Verse_Ch: 46:11 埃及的处女阿，可以上基列取乳香去；你虽多服良药，总是徒然，不得治好。 ###EN### Go up to Gilead and take balm, O virgin daughter of Egypt. In vain you have used many medicines-There is no healing for you.
Verse_Ch: 46:12 列国听见你的羞辱，大地满了你的哀声；勇士与勇士彼此相碰，一齐跌倒。 ###EN### The nations have heard of your disgrace, And your cry has filled the earth; For mighty man has stumbled against mighty man; Both of them have fallen together.
Verse_Ch: 46:13 耶和华对申言者耶利米所说的话，论到巴比伦王尼布甲尼撒要来攻击埃及地： ###EN### The word which Jehovah spoke to Jeremiah the prophet about the coming of Nebuchadrezzar the king of Babylon to strike the land of Egypt:
Verse_Ch: 46:14 你们要传扬在埃及，宣告在密夺，报告在挪弗、答比匿，说，要站稳，自作准备；因为刀剑在你四围施行吞灭。 ###EN### Declare in Egypt, and proclaim in Migdol; Proclaim also in Memphis and in Tahpanhes. Say, Take your stand, and prepare yourself; For the sword has devoured all around you.
Verse_Ch: 46:15 你的壮士为何仆倒？他站立不住，因为耶和华将他推倒了。 ###EN### Why are your mighty men prostrate? He does not stand, because Jehovah has cast him down.
Verse_Ch: 46:16 他使多人绊跌；他们也彼此撞倒，说，起来罢，我们回到本民和出生地去，好躲避欺压者的刀剑。 ###EN### He made many stumble; A man even fell against his neighbor; And they said, Arise and let us return To our own people and to the land of our birth, Away from the sword of the oppressor.
Verse_Ch: 46:17 他们在那里喊叫说，埃及王法老不过是哄嚷的声音；他已错过所定的时候了。 ###EN### There they cried, Pharaoh, the king of Egypt, is but a noise; He has let the appointed time pass by.
Verse_Ch: 46:18 名为万军之耶和华的王说，我指着我的生存起誓，尼布甲尼撒必来，他的气势必像他泊在众山之中，像迦密在海边一样。 ###EN### As I live, says the King, Whose name is Jehovah of hosts, Surely as Tabor is among the mountains, And Carmel is by the sea, so he will come.
Verse_Ch: 46:19 埃及的女子阿，居民哪，要预备掳去时所用的物件；因为挪弗必成为荒场，且被烧毁，无人居住。 ###EN### Prepare for yourself baggage for captivity, O inhabitant, O daughter of Egypt; For Memphis will become a waste, And it will be burned, without inhabitant.
Verse_Ch: 46:20 埃及是肥美的母牛犊；但出于北方的牛 来到她身上了。 ###EN### Egypt is a beautiful heifer; A gadfly from the north has come on her.
Verse_Ch: 46:21 其中的雇勇，好像圈里的肥牛犊；他们也转身退后，一齐逃跑，站立不住；因为他们遭难的日子，追讨的时候，已经临到。 ###EN### Also her hired men in her midst Are like fattened calves. But they have also turned back; They have fled together; they did not stand. For the day of their calamity has come on them, The time of their visitation.
Verse_Ch: 46:22 她的声音好像蛇行的声音一样；敌人要成队前来，如砍伐树木的拿斧子来攻击她。 ###EN### Her sound is like that of a serpent going away; For they go forth in force, And with axes they come against her, Like those who fell trees.
Verse_Ch: 46:23 耶和华说，埃及的树林，虽然穿越不过，敌人却要砍伐；因他们多于蝗虫，不可胜数。 ###EN### They will cut down her forest, declares Jehovah, Although it is impenetrable; For they are more numerous than locusts And are without number.
Verse_Ch: 46:24 埃及的女子蒙受羞辱，交在北方的民手中。 ###EN### The daughter of Egypt is put to shame; She is given into the hand of a people from the north.
Verse_Ch: 46:25 万军之耶和华以色列的神说，我必惩罚挪的亚扪神、法老、并埃及、与埃及的神、以及埃及的诸王，就是法老和倚靠他的人。 ###EN### Jehovah of hosts, the God of Israel, says, I will punish Amon of No and Pharaoh and Egypt and her gods and her kings, even Pharaoh and those who trust in him.
Verse_Ch: 46:26 我要将他们交付寻索他们性命之人的手，就是巴比伦王尼布甲尼撒与他臣仆的手；此后埃及必再有人居住，与从前一样；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### And I will give them into the hand of those who seek their life, even into the hand of Nebuchadrezzar the king of Babylon and into the hand of his servants; and afterward she will be inhabited as in the days of old, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 46:27 至于你，我的仆人雅各阿，不要惧怕；以色列阿，不要惊惶。因为我要从远方拯救你，从你后裔被掳到之地拯救他们；雅各必回来得享平静安宁， 无人使他害怕。 ###EN### But as for you, O Jacob My servant, do not fear; And do not be dismayed, O Israel. For indeed I will save you from afar And your seed from the land of their captivity; And Jacob will return and be undisturbed And at ease, and no one will frighten him.
Verse_Ch: 46:28 我的仆人雅各阿，不要惧怕；因我与你同在；我要将我所赶你到的那些国灭绝净尽；却不将你灭绝净尽，倒要适度管教你，绝不能不罚你；这是耶 和华说的。 ###EN### As for you, O Jacob My servant, do not fear, declares Jehovah, For I am with you; For I will make a full end of all the nations To which I have driven you; Yet I will not make a full end of you, But will correct you in measure And will by no means leave you unpunished.
Chapter_Header: 47
Verse_Ch: 47:1 法老攻击迦萨之先，有耶和华论非利士人的话临到申言者耶利米。 ###EN### The word of Jehovah that came to Jeremiah the prophet concerning the Philistines before Pharaoh struck Gaza.
Verse_Ch: 47:2 耶和华如此说，看哪，有水从北方涨发，成为泛滥的河，要漫过那地和其中所有的，并城和其中所住的；人必呼喊，那地的居民都必哀号。 ###EN### Thus says Jehovah, See, waters are rising up from the north And will become an overflowing stream; And they will overflow the land and all that fills it, The city and those who dwell in it; And men will cry out, And every inhabitant of the land will howl.
Verse_Ch: 47:3 因敌人壮马蹄跳的响声，和战车隆隆，车轮轰轰，为父的手就发软，不回头看顾儿女， ###EN### At the sound of the stamping of the hooves of his stallions, At the rushing of his chariots, at the rumbling of his wheels, The fathers will not turn back for their children, Because of the feebleness of their hands,
Verse_Ch: 47:4 因为日子将到，要毁灭一切非利士人，剪除推罗、西顿一切余剩的帮助者；原来耶和华必毁灭非利士人，就是迦斐托海岛余剩的人。 ###EN### Because of the day which is coming, To destroy all the Philistines, To cut off from Tyre and Sidon Every helper who survives; For Jehovah will destroy the Philistines, The remnant of the coastland of Caphtor.
Verse_Ch: 47:5 迦萨成了光秃；亚实基伦已被剪除；山谷中余剩的人哪，你用刀划身，要到几时呢？ ###EN### Baldness has come upon Gaza; Ashkelon has been cut off. O remnant of their valley, How long will you cut yourself?
Verse_Ch: 47:6 哀哉，耶和华的刀剑哪，你到几时才止息呢？你要入鞘，静止不动。 ###EN### Alas, O sword of Jehovah, How long until you are quiet? Put yourself into your sheath; Rest and be still.
Verse_Ch: 47:7 耶和华既吩咐攻击亚实基伦和海边之地，祂已经派定，焉能止息呢？ ###EN### How can it be quiet, When Jehovah has commanded it? Against Ashkelon and against the seacoast-There He has appointed it.
Chapter_Header: 48
Verse_Ch: 48:1 论摩押：万军之耶和华以色列的神如此说，尼波有祸了，因遭毁灭；基列亭蒙羞被攻取；高台蒙羞被毁坏。 ###EN### Concerning Moab: Thus says Jehovah of hosts, the God of Israel: Woe to Nebo, for it is destroyed; Kiriathaim is put to shame; it is captured; The lofty retreat is put to shame and dismayed.
Verse_Ch: 48:2 摩押不再被称赞；有人在希实本设计谋害她，说，来罢，我们将她剪除，使她不再成国。玛得缅哪，你也必默默无声；刀剑必紧随着你。 ###EN### The praise of Moab is no more; In Heshbon they have devised evil against her, saying: Come and let us cut her off from being a nation. You also, O Madmen, will be brought to silence; A sword will go after you.
Verse_Ch: 48:3 从何罗念有哀声喊说，荒凉和大毁坏！ ###EN### The sound of a cry from Horonaim, Desolation and great destruction!
Verse_Ch: 48:4 摩押毁坏了；她的孩童发哀声，使人听见。 ###EN### Moab is destroyed; Her young have caused a cry to be heard.
Verse_Ch: 48:5 人上鲁希坡随走随哭；因为在何罗念的下坡，听见毁坏的哀声。 ###EN### For by the ascent of Luhith Continual weeping will go up; For by the descent of Horonaim They have heard the distress of the cry of destruction.
Verse_Ch: 48:6 你们要奔逃，自救性命，要像旷野的灌木。 ###EN### Flee, save your life, And be like a shrub in the wilderness.
Verse_Ch: 48:7 你因倚靠自己所作的和自己的财宝，你也必被攻取；基抹和属他的祭司、首领，也要一同被迁徙出去。 ###EN### For because of your trust in your works and in your treasures, You also will be captured; And Chemosh will go forth into exile; His priests and his princes together.
Verse_Ch: 48:8 行毁坏的必来到各城，并无一城逃脱；山谷也必败亡，平原必被毁坏；正如耶和华所说的。 ###EN### And a destroyer will come to every city, And no city will escape; The valley will also perish, And the plateau will be destroyed, As Jehovah has said.
Verse_Ch: 48:9 要将翅膀给摩押，使她可以飞去；她的城邑必至荒凉，无人居住。 ###EN### Give wings to Moab, That she may fly and go away; And her cities will become a waste, Without inhabitant in them.
Verse_Ch: 48:10 松散怠慢为耶和华作工的，必受咒诅；禁止自己刀剑不经血的，必受咒诅。 ###EN### Cursed is he who does the work of Jehovah negligently, And cursed is he who keeps his sword from blood.
Verse_Ch: 48:11 摩押自幼年以来，常享安逸，如酒在渣滓上澄清，没有从这器皿倒在那器皿里，也未曾被迁徙；因此，他的原味尚存，香气未变。 ###EN### Moab has been at ease from his youth; And he is settled on his lees And has not been emptied from vessel to vessel; Nor has he gone into exile. Therefore his taste remains in him, And his scent is not changed.
Verse_Ch: 48:12 耶和华说，因此日子将到，我必打发倒酒的往他那里去，将他倒出来；倒空他的器皿，打碎他的坛子。 ###EN### Therefore indeed, days are coming, declares Jehovah, when I will send pourers to him, and they will pour and empty his vessels and shatter his jars.
Verse_Ch: 48:13 摩押必因基抹羞愧，像以色列家从前因他们所倚靠的伯特利羞愧一样。 ###EN### And Moab will be ashamed of Chemosh, as the house of Israel was ashamed of Bethel, their confidence.
Verse_Ch: 48:14 你们怎么说，我们是勇士，是有勇力打仗的人呢？ ###EN### How can you say, We are mighty men And valiant men for war?
Verse_Ch: 48:15 摩押毁灭了；他的城邑如烟上腾；他所特选的少年人，下去遭了杀戮；这是名为万军之耶和华的王说的。 ###EN### Moab has been destroyed, And its cities have gone up in smoke, And its choice young men have gone down to slaughter, Declares the King, whose name is Jehovah of hosts.
Verse_Ch: 48:16 摩押的灾祸临近，他的苦难速速来到。 ###EN### The calamity of Moab is near to coming, And his affliction hastens quickly.
Verse_Ch: 48:17 凡在他四围的，和认识他名的，你们都要为他悲伤，说，那有力量的杖，和那荣美的棍，何竟折断！ ###EN### Lament for him, all who are around him And all who know his name; Say, How the strong rod is broken, The glorious staff.
Verse_Ch: 48:18 住在底本的女子阿，要从你荣耀的位上下来，坐受干渴；因毁灭摩押的上来攻击你；他毁坏了你的保障。 ###EN### Come down from glory and sit in thirst, O daughter who dwells in Dibon, For the destroyer of Moab has come up against you; He has destroyed your strongholds.
Verse_Ch: 48:19 亚罗珥的居民哪，要站在路旁观望；问逃避的男人和逃脱的女人，说，是什么事呢？ ###EN### Stand by the way and watch, O inhabitant of Aroer; Ask him who flees and her who escapes, And say, What has happened?
Verse_Ch: 48:20 摩押因毁坏蒙羞。你们要哀号呼喊；要在亚嫩报告，说，摩押毁灭了。 ###EN### Moab is put to shame, for it is shattered. Howl and cry out; Declare in Arnon That Moab is devastated.
Verse_Ch: 48:21 审判临到高原之地的何伦、雅杂、米法押、 ###EN### And judgment has come upon the land of the Plateau, on Holon and on Jahzah and on Mephaath
Verse_Ch: 48:22 底本、尼波、伯低比拉太音、 ###EN### And on Dibon and on Nebo and on Beth-diblathaim
Verse_Ch: 48:23 基列亭、伯迦末、伯米恩、 ###EN### And on Kiriathaim and on Beth-gamul and on Beth-meon
Verse_Ch: 48:24 加略、波斯拉、和摩押地远近一切的城邑。 ###EN### And on Kerioth and on Bozrah and on all the cities of the land of Moab, far and near.
Verse_Ch: 48:25 摩押的角砍断了，摩押的膀臂折断了；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### The horn of Moab is cut off, and his arm is broken, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 48:26 你们要使摩押沉醉，因他向耶和华夸大；他要在自己所吐之物中打滚，又要被人嗤笑。 ###EN### Make him drunk, because he magnified himself against Jehovah; so Moab will wallow in his vomit and will also be in derision.
Verse_Ch: 48:27 你岂不曾嗤笑以色列么？他岂是在盗贼中间发现的么？你每逢提到他便摇头。 ###EN### For was not Israel a derision to you? Or was he found among thieves? For as often as you speak of him, you shake your head.
Verse_Ch: 48:28 摩押的居民哪，要离开城邑，住在岩石里，像鸽子在坑口上搭窝。 ###EN### Leave the cities and dwell in the rock, O inhabitants of Moab, And be like a dove who nests On the sides of the mouth of the pit.
Verse_Ch: 48:29 我们听说摩押的骄傲，是极其骄傲；听说过他的狂傲、骄傲、狂妄、并心中的高傲。 ###EN### We have heard of the pride of Moab-He is extremely proud-Of his loftiness and his pride and his arrogance And of the haughtiness of his heart.
Verse_Ch: 48:30 耶和华说，我知道他的忿怒，他夸大的话是不正确的，是一无所成的。 ###EN### I know of his insolence, declares Jehovah; His boastings are all untrue; They have accomplished nothing.
Verse_Ch: 48:31 因此，我要为摩押哀号，为全摩押呼喊；人必为吉珥哈列设人哀叹。 ###EN### Therefore I will wail for Moab, I will even cry out for all Moab; There will be mourning for the men of Kir-heres.
Verse_Ch: 48:32 西比玛的葡萄树阿，我为你哀哭甚于雅谢人的哀哭；你的枝子蔓延过海，直达到海，达到雅谢；那行毁灭的，已经临到你夏天的果子，和你所摘的 葡萄。 ###EN### With more than the weeping of Jazer I will weep for you, O vine of Sibmah. Your shoots have crossed over to the sea; They have reached as far as the sea, to Jazer; On your summer fruit and on your vintage The destroyer has fallen.
Verse_Ch: 48:33 肥田和摩押地的喜乐欢腾，都被夺去。我使酒醡的酒绝流，无人踹酒，欢呼收成；收割的欢呼成了没有收割的喊声。 ###EN### Rejoicing and exultation are taken away From the fruited field and from the land of Moab. And I have caused the wine from the wine presses to cease; No one will tread them with the harvest shout; The harvest shout will be no harvest shout.
Verse_Ch: 48:34 希实本人发的哀声，达到以利亚利，直达到雅杂，从琐珥达到何罗念，直到伊基拉施利施亚；因为连宁林的水，也必干涸。 ###EN### From the cry of Heshbon as far as Elealeh, even as far as Jahaz, they have uttered their voice, from Zoar as far as Horonaim and to Eglath-shelishiyah; for even the waters of Nimrim will become a devastation.
Verse_Ch: 48:35 耶和华说，我必在摩押地，使那上邱坛献祭的，和向他的神烧香的，都断绝了。 ###EN### And I will bring to an end in Moab the one who offers up in high places and burns incense to his gods, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 48:36 所以我的心为摩押哀鸣如箫，我的心为吉珥哈列设人也是如此；故此摩押所积的财富，都灭没了。 ###EN### Therefore My heart will moan for Moab like flutes; for the men of Kir-heres My heart will also moan like flutes. As a result, the abundance he has produced has perished.
Verse_Ch: 48:37 各人头上光秃，胡须剃净，手有划伤，腰束麻布。 ###EN### For every head is bald, and every beard is shaved off; there are cuts on all the hands, and sackcloth on the loins.
Verse_Ch: 48:38 在摩押的各房顶上和宽阔处，处处有人哀哭；因我打碎摩押，好像打碎没有人要的器皿；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### On all the roofs of Moab and in her open squares there is wailing everywhere, for I have broken Moab like a vessel which no one desires, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 48:39 摩押遭了何等的毁坏！他们哀号，摩押何等羞愧的转背！因此，摩押必令四围的众人嗤笑、惊骇。 ###EN### How it is shattered! they howl. How Moab has turned his back in shame! So Moab has become a derision and a terror to all who are around him.
Verse_Ch: 48:40 耶和华如此说，必有一人如大鹰扑下，展开翅膀攻击摩押。 ###EN### For thus says Jehovah, One will swoop down like an eagle And spread its wings against Moab.
Verse_Ch: 48:41 加略被攻取，保障也被占据；到那日，摩押勇士的心必疼痛，如临产妇人的心一样。 ###EN### Kerioth is captured, And the strongholds are seized, And the heart of the mighty men of Moab in that day Will be like the heart of a woman in labor.
Verse_Ch: 48:42 摩押必被毁灭，不再成一民，因他向耶和华夸大。 ###EN### And Moab will be destroyed from being a people, Because he magnified himself against Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 48:43 耶和华说，摩押的居民哪，恐惧、陷坑、网罗，都临及你。 ###EN### Dread, pit, and snare Are upon you, O inhabitant of Moab, Declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 48:44 躲避恐惧的，要坠入陷坑；从陷坑上来的，要被网罗缠住；因我必使追讨之年临到摩押；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### He who flees from dread Will fall into the pit, And he who comes up out of the pit Will be taken in the snare; For I will bring upon her, upon Moab, The year of their punishment, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 48:45 躲避的人，无力的站在希实本的荫下；因为有火从希实本发出，有火焰出于西宏中间，烧尽摩押的角落，和哄嚷人的头顶。 ###EN### In the shadow of Heshbon Those who flee stand without strength; For fire has gone forth from Heshbon And a flame from the midst of Sihon; And it has consumed the corner of Moab And the top of the head of the sons of tumult.
Verse_Ch: 48:46 摩押阿，你有祸了！属基抹的民灭亡了，因你的众子都被掳去，你的众女也被掳去。 ###EN### Woe to you, O Moab! The people of Chemosh have perished, For your sons have been taken captive, And your daughters have gone into captivity.
Verse_Ch: 48:47 耶和华说，但到末后的日子，我要使被掳的摩押人归回。摩押受审判的话到此为止。 ###EN### But I will turn again the captivity of Moab In the last days, declares Jehovah. Thus far is the judgment of Moab.
Chapter_Header: 49
Verse_Ch: 49:1 论亚扪人：耶和华如此说，以色列没有儿子么？没有后嗣么？玛勒堪为何得迦得之地为业呢？属他的民为何住迦得的城邑呢？ ###EN### Concerning the children of Ammon: Thus says Jehovah, Does Israel have no sons? Or has he no heir? Why has Malcam possessed Gad, And why do his people dwell in his cities?
Verse_Ch: 49:2 耶和华说，因此日子将到，我必使人听见打仗的呐喊，是攻击亚扪人拉巴的呐喊。拉巴要成为乱堆；其乡村要被火焚烧；先前赶出以色列的，这时以 色列要赶出他们；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### Therefore indeed, days are coming, declares Jehovah, When I will cause the alarm of war to be heard Against Rabbah of the children of Ammon. And it will become a mound of desolation, And its villages will be burned with fire. And Israel will dispossess those who dispossess him, Says Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 49:3 希实本哪，你要哀号，因为艾城已被毁灭；拉巴的女子阿，要呼喊。要以麻布束腰，要哭号，在围篱内跑来跑去；因玛勒堪和属他的祭司、首领，要 一同被迁徙。 ###EN### Howl, O Heshbon, for Ai has been destroyed; Cry out, O daughters of Rabbah. Gird yourselves with sackcloth and wail, And run to and fro among the enclosures; For Malcam will go into exile, Together with his priests and his princes.
Verse_Ch: 49:4 背道的女子阿，你倚靠自己的财宝，说，谁会来攻击我呢？你为何夸耀自己的山谷呢？你的山谷必如水流失。 ###EN### Why do you boast in your valleys? Your valley is flowing away, O apostate daughter, Who trusts in her treasures, saying, Who will come against me?
Verse_Ch: 49:5 主万军之耶和华说，我要使恐吓从四围的众人中临到你们；你们必被赶出，各往各方，没有人收聚逃民。 ###EN### I will bring dread upon you, Declares the Lord Jehovah of hosts, From all around you; And each one will be driven out headlong, And no one will gather him who flees.
Verse_Ch: 49:6 但后来我要使被掳的亚扪人归回；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### But afterward I will turn again The captivity of the children of Ammon, Declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 49:7 论以东：万军之耶和华如此说，提幔中再没有智慧么？聪明人不再有谋略么？他们的智慧耗尽了么？ ###EN### Concerning Edom: Thus says Jehovah of hosts, Is there no more wisdom in Teman? Has counsel perished from those who understand? Is their wisdom spent?
Verse_Ch: 49:8 底但的居民哪，要转身逃跑，住在隐密处；因为我向以扫追讨的时候，必使灾祸临到他。 ###EN### Flee, turn back, dwell in hidden places, O inhabitants of Dedan, For I will bring the calamity of Esau upon him At the time I visit him.
Verse_Ch: 49:9 摘葡萄的若来到你这里，岂不剩下些葡萄么？盗贼若夜间来，岂不是只毁坏到够了么？ ###EN### If the grape gatherers came to you, Would they not leave gleanings? If thieves came by night, Would they not destroy only enough for themselves?
Verse_Ch: 49:10 我却剥光以扫，显出他的隐密处；他不能掩藏自己。他的后裔、弟兄、邻舍，尽都毁灭，他也归于无有。 ###EN### But I have stripped Esau bare; I have exposed his secret places, And he is not able to conceal himself. His seed and his brothers are destroyed, And his neighbors and he are no more.
Verse_Ch: 49:11 你撇下孤儿，我必使他们存活；你的寡妇可以信靠我。 ###EN### Leave your orphans behind; I will preserve them alive, And let your widows trust in Me.
Verse_Ch: 49:12 耶和华如此说，原来判定不该喝那杯的，一定要喝。你能尽免刑罚么？你不能免罚，一定要喝。 ###EN### For thus says Jehovah, Those whose judgment was not to drink the cup will certainly drink it. And will you by any means be left unpunished? You will not be left unpunished, for you will certainly drink it.
Verse_Ch: 49:13 耶和华说，我指着自己起誓，波斯拉必成为荒废、羞辱、咒诅，并且荒凉；她的一切城邑，必成为永远的荒场。 ###EN### For I have sworn by Myself, declares Jehovah, that Bozrah will become a waste, a reproach, a ruin and a curse; and all her cities will become eternal desolations.
Verse_Ch: 49:14 我从耶和华那里听见信息，并有使者被差往列国去，说，你们聚集来攻击以东，起来争战。 ###EN### I have heard a report from Jehovah, And an envoy is sent among the nations, saying, Gather yourselves together, and come against her, And arise for war.
Verse_Ch: 49:15 因为我使你在列国中为最小，在人中间被藐视。 ###EN### For, indeed, I have made you small among the nations, Despised among men.
Verse_Ch: 49:16 住在磐石穴中，据守高冈的阿，你的威吓，你心中的狂傲，欺骗了你。你虽如鹰高高搭窝，我必从那里拉下你来；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### Your terribleness, the pride of your heart, Has beguiled you, O you who dwell in the clefts of the rock, Who grasp the height of the hill. Though you make your nest as high as an eagle's, I will bring you down from there, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 49:17 以东必令人惊骇；凡经过的人都必惊骇，又嗤笑她一切的创伤。 ###EN### And Edom will become an astonishment; everyone who passes by her will be astonished and will hiss at all her wounds.
Verse_Ch: 49:18 耶和华说，必无人住在那里，也无世人在其中寄居，就像所多玛、蛾摩拉、和邻近的城邑倾覆一样。 ###EN### As when Sodom and Gomorrah were overthrown with its neighbors, says Jehovah, no one will dwell there, nor will a son of man sojourn in her.
Verse_Ch: 49:19 看哪，必有一人像狮子从约但河边的丛林上来，攻击坚固的居所；转眼之间，我要使以东人逃跑离开她；谁蒙拣选，我就派谁治理她。谁能像我呢？ 谁能给我定规日期呢？谁是那能在我面前站立的牧人呢？ ###EN### Indeed, one will come up like a lion from the majesty of the Jordan against a secure habitation, for I will suddenly make them run away from her; and whoever is chosen I will appoint over her. For who is like Me? And who can appoint Me a time? And who is that shepherd who can stand before Me?
Verse_Ch: 49:20 所以你们要听耶和华攻击以东所设的谋略，和祂攻击提幔居民所定的意念：仇敌定要将他们羊群中微小的拉去；祂定要使他们的居所荒凉。 ###EN### Therefore hear the counsel of Jehovah, which He purposed against Edom, and His thoughts, which He has thought against the inhabitants of Teman: Surely they will drag them off, the little ones of the flock; surely He will make their habitation a desolation because of them.
Verse_Ch: 49:21 因他们仆倒的声音，地就震动。人在红海那里，听见了呼喊的声音。 ###EN### The earth quaked at the sound of their fall. There is a cry; the sound of it has been heard in the Red Sea.
Verse_Ch: 49:22 祂必如大鹰飞起扑下，展开翅膀攻击波斯拉；到那日，以东勇士的心必疼痛，如临产妇人的心一样。 ###EN### Indeed, He will mount up and swoop down like an eagle, and spread out His wings over Bozrah; and the heart of the mighty men of Edom in that day will be like the heart of a woman in labor.
Verse_Ch: 49:23 论大马色：哈马和亚珥拔蒙羞，因为他们听见凶恶的消息。他们的心融化；海上有忧虑，不得平静。 ###EN### Concerning Damascus: Hamath and Arpad are put to shame Because they have heard an evil report. They melt; anxiety is on the sea; It cannot be quiet.
Verse_Ch: 49:24 大马色发软，转身逃跑；恐慌将她捉住，痛苦忧愁将她抓住，如正在生产的妇人一样。 ###EN### Damascus has become feeble; She has turned to flee, And panic has taken hold of her; Pain and anguish seize her, Like a woman giving birth.
Verse_Ch: 49:25 我所称赞的城、所喜乐的镇，为何没有被撇弃呢？ ###EN### How the city of praise is not forsaken, The town of My joy.
Verse_Ch: 49:26 因此，她的少年人必仆倒在街上；当那日，一切兵丁必默默无声；这是万军之耶和华说的。 ###EN### Therefore her young men will fall in her open squares, And all the men of war will be silenced in that day, declares Jehovah of hosts.
Verse_Ch: 49:27 我必在大马色城墙使火着起，烧灭便哈达的宫殿。 ###EN### And I will set fire to the wall of Damascus, And it will consume the palaces of Ben-hadad.
Verse_Ch: 49:28 论巴比伦王尼布甲尼撒所攻打的基达，和夏琐的诸国：耶和华如此说，起来，上基达去，毁灭东方人。 ###EN### Concerning Kedar and the kingdoms of Hazor, which Nebuchadrezzar the king of Babylon struck down: Thus says Jehovah: Arise, go up against Kedar, And destroy the children of the east.
Verse_Ch: 49:29 他们的帐棚和羊群，都要夺去；要将幔子和一切器皿并骆驼，为自己掠去；他们要彼此喊着说，四围都有惊吓！ ###EN### And they will take away their tents and their flocks; Their curtains and all their vessels And their camels they will carry away for themselves, And they will call out to one another, Terror is on every side!
Verse_Ch: 49:30 耶和华说，夏琐的居民哪，要逃奔远方，住在隐密处；因为巴比伦王尼布甲尼撒设计谋害你们，定策略攻击你们。 ###EN### Flee, wander far away, dwell in hidden places, O inhabitants of Hazor, declares Jehovah; For Nebuchadrezzar the king of Babylon Has taken counsel against you And has devised a plan against you.
Verse_Ch: 49:31 耶和华说，起来，上安居无虑的国那里去；他们是无门无闩，独自居住的。 ###EN### Arise, go up against a nation without care, One that dwells securely, declares Jehovah. It has no gates and bars; They dwell alone.
Verse_Ch: 49:32 他们的骆驼必成为掠物，他们众多的牲畜必成为掳物；我必将剃周围胡须的人分散各方，使灾祸从四围临到他们；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### And their camels will become plunder, And the multitude of their livestock spoil; And I will scatter those who cut the corners of their beards into every wind, And I will bring their calamity from every side of them, Declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 49:33 夏琐必成为野狗的住处，永远荒凉；必无人住在那里，也无世人在其中寄居。 ###EN### And Hazor will become a habitation of jackals, An eternal desolation; No one will dwell there; Neither will a son of man sojourn in it.
Verse_Ch: 49:34 犹大王西底家登基的时候，耶和华论以拦的话临到申言者耶利米，说， ###EN### The word of Jehovah which came to Jeremiah the prophet concerning Elam, in the beginning of the reign of Zedekiah the king of Judah, saying,
Verse_Ch: 49:35 万军之耶和华如此说，我必折断以拦人的弓，就是他们勇力的主要部分。 ###EN### Thus says Jehovah of hosts, I am about to break the bow of Elam, The chief part of their might.
Verse_Ch: 49:36 我要使四风从天的四方刮来，临到以拦人，将他们分散到四方；从以拦被赶出的人，必没有一国不到的。 ###EN### And I will bring against Elam four winds From the four ends of the heavens, And I will scatter them into all these winds, And there will not be a nation To which those who are driven out from Elam will not go.
Verse_Ch: 49:37 耶和华说，我必使以拦人在仇敌和寻索其命的人面前惊惶；我也必使灾祸，就是我的烈怒，临到他们；又必打发刀剑追杀他们，直到将他们灭尽。 ###EN### And I will cause Elam to be dismayed before their enemies And before those who seek their life; And I will bring evil upon them, Even My burning anger, declares Jehovah. And I will send the sword after them, Until I make an end of them.
Verse_Ch: 49:38 我要在以拦设立我的宝座，从那里除灭君王和首领；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### And I will set My throne in Elam, And I will destroy king and princes from there, Declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 49:39 但在末后的日子，我还要使被掳的以拦人归回；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### But in the last days, I will turn again the captivity of Elam, Declares Jehovah.
Chapter_Header: 50
Verse_Ch: 50:1 耶和华藉申言者耶利米论巴比伦和迦勒底人之地所说的话： ###EN### The word which Jehovah spoke concerning Babylon, concerning the land of the Chaldeans, through Jeremiah the prophet:
Verse_Ch: 50:2 你们要在万国中传扬报告，竖立旌旗；要报告，不可隐瞒，说，巴比伦被攻取，彼勒蒙羞，米罗达惊惶；巴比伦的神像都蒙羞，她的偶像都惊惶。 ###EN### Declare among the nations and proclaim; Lift up a banner, proclaim it. Do not conceal it, but say, Babylon is captured; Bel is put to shame; Merodach is shattered; Her images are put to shame; Her idols are dismayed.
Verse_Ch: 50:3 因有一国从北方上来攻击她，使她的地荒凉，无人居住；连人带牲畜，都逃走了。 ###EN### For a nation has come up against her from the north; It will make her land a waste, And there will be no inhabitant in it; Both man and beast have fled; they are gone away.
Verse_Ch: 50:4 耶和华说，当那些日子，那时候，以色列人要和犹大人同来，随走随哭，寻求耶和华他们的神。 ###EN### In those days and at that time, declares Jehovah, The children of Israel will come, Both they and the children of Judah together; They will go along with weeping as they go, And they will seek Jehovah their God.
Verse_Ch: 50:5 他们必询问去锡安的路，又面向这里，说，来罢，我们要凭永远不忘的约，与耶和华联结。 ###EN### They will ask for the way to Zion With their faces toward it, saying: Come and let us join ourselves to Jehovah In an eternal covenant that will not be forgotten.
Verse_Ch: 50:6 我的百姓成了迷失的羊；他们的牧人使他们走错了路，使他们流落山上；他们从大山走到小山，竟忘了安歇之处。 ###EN### My people are lost sheep; Their shepherds have led them astray; They have made them turn aside on the mountains; They have gone from mountain to hill; They have forgotten their resting place.
Verse_Ch: 50:7 凡遇见他们的，就把他们吞灭；他们的敌人说，我们没有罪，因为他们得罪了那作公义居所的耶和华，就是他们列祖所盼望的耶和华。 ###EN### All who found them have devoured them, And their adversaries have said, We are not guilty, Because they have sinned against Jehovah, The habitation of righteousness, Even Jehovah, the hope of their fathers.
Verse_Ch: 50:8 你们要从巴比伦中间逃走，从迦勒底人之地出去，像羊群前面走的公山羊。 ###EN### Flee from the midst of Babylon, And go out from the land of the Chaldeans, And be as male goats Before the flock.
Verse_Ch: 50:9 因我必激动联合的大国，从北方之地上来攻击巴比伦；他们要摆阵攻击她，她必从那里被攻取。他们的箭，好像善战勇士的箭，无一徒然返回。 ###EN### For I am about to stir up and bring up against Babylon An assembly of great nations from the land of the north; And they will set themselves in array against her, And she will be taken captive from there. Their arrows will be like those of an expert mighty man; None will return empty-handed.
Verse_Ch: 50:10 迦勒底必成为掠物；凡掳掠她的都必心满意足；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### And Chaldea will become spoil; All those who spoil her will be satisfied, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 50:11 抢夺我产业的阿，因你们喜乐欢腾，因你们欢跳像踹谷的母牛犊，又发嘶声像壮马， ###EN### Because you rejoiced, because you exulted, O you who plunder My inheritance, Because you spring about as a threshing heifer, And you neigh like stallions,
Verse_Ch: 50:12 你们的母亲巴比伦就极其抱愧，生你们的必然蒙羞；她被列在诸国之末，沦为旷野、旱地、沙漠。 ###EN### Your mother has been greatly ashamed; She who bore you has become a reproach: Indeed, she has become the last of the nations, A wilderness, a dry land and a desert.
Verse_Ch: 50:13 因耶和华的忿怒，她必无人居住，要全然荒凉；凡经过巴比伦的，都必惊骇，又嗤笑她一切的创伤。 ###EN### Because of the wrath of Jehovah she will not be inhabited, But she will become a complete desolation; For every one who passes by Babylon will be astonished And will hiss at all her wounds.
Verse_Ch: 50:14 所有拉弓的，你们要在巴比伦的四围摆阵，射箭攻击她；不要爱惜箭枝，因她得罪了耶和华。 ###EN### Set yourselves in array against Babylon all around, All those who bend the bow; Shoot at her; spare no arrow; Because she has sinned against Jehovah;
Verse_Ch: 50:15 你们要四围呐喊攻击她。她已经投降；她的外郭坍塌了，城墙拆毁了；因为这是耶和华报仇的事；你们要向巴比伦报仇，她怎样待人，也要怎样待 她。 ###EN### Raise a shout against her all around. She has surrendered; her buttresses have fallen, Her walls have been torn down; For this is the vengeance of Jehovah: Take vengeance on her; As she has done, so do to her.
Verse_Ch: 50:16 你们要将巴比伦撒种的和收割时拿镰刀的，都剪除了；他们各人因怕欺压者的刀剑，必归回本族，逃到本土。 ###EN### Cut off the sower from Babylon, And the one who handles a sickle in the time of harvest; Because of the sword of the oppressor Each one will turn to his people, And each one flee to his own land.
Verse_Ch: 50:17 以色列是打散的羊，狮子把他赶逐出去了。首先是亚述王将他吞灭，末后是巴比伦王尼布甲尼撒将他的骨头啃断。 ###EN### Israel is a scattered sheep; Lions have driven him away. First the king of Assyria devoured him, and last this Nebuchadrezzar the king of Babylon has gnawed his bones.
Verse_Ch: 50:18 所以万军之耶和华以色列的神如此说，我必惩罚巴比伦王和他的地，像我从前惩罚亚述王一样。 ###EN### Therefore thus says Jehovah of hosts, the God of Israel: I will punish the king of Babylon and his land, as I punished the king of Assyria.
Verse_Ch: 50:19 我必再领以色列回他的居所；他必在迦密和巴珊得喂养，又在以法莲山地和基列境内，魂得饱足。 ###EN### And I will bring Israel back to his habitation, And he will feed on Carmel and Bashan, And in the hill country of Ephraim and in Gilead He will satisfy his soul.
Verse_Ch: 50:20 耶和华说，当那些日子，那时候，虽寻以色列的罪孽，却一无所得；虽寻犹大的罪，也一无所见；因为我所留下的人，我必赦免。 ###EN### In those days and at that time, declares Jehovah, The iniquity of Israel will be sought, but there will be none; And the sin of Judah, but it will not be found; For I will forgive those whom I will leave as a remnant.
Verse_Ch: 50:21 耶和华说，上去攻击她，攻击米拉大翁之地，又攻击比割的居民。要摧残毁灭净尽，照我所吩咐你的一切去行。 ###EN### Go up against her, against the land of Merathaim And against the inhabitants of Pekod. Desolate and utterly destroy them, declares Jehovah, And do according to all that I commanded you.
Verse_Ch: 50:22 这地有打仗和大毁坏的响声。 ###EN### The sound of war is in the land, And great destruction.
Verse_Ch: 50:23 全地的大锤，何竟砍断破毁！巴比伦在列国中，何竟令人惊骇！ ###EN### How the hammer of the whole earth Is cut down and broken! How Babylon has become an astonishment Among the nations!
Verse_Ch: 50:24 巴比伦哪，我为你设下网罗，你被缠住却不自知；你被寻着，也被捉住，因为你与耶和华争战。 ###EN### I have set a snare for you, and you also have been taken captive, O Babylon, and you did not know; You were found, and you also were seized, Because you engaged in war with Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 50:25 耶和华已经开了武库，拿出祂恼恨的兵器，因为这是主万军之耶和华的工作，要攻击迦勒底人之地。 ###EN### Jehovah has opened His armory And has brought out the weapons of His wrath, For this is the work of the Lord Jehovah of hosts Against the land of the Chaldeans.
Verse_Ch: 50:26 你们要从四围来攻击她，开她的仓廪，将她堆如高堆，毁灭净尽，丝毫不留。 ###EN### Come against her from every side; Open her granaries. Pile her up like heaps; Destroy her utterly; Let nothing of her remain.
Verse_Ch: 50:27 要杀她的一切公牛，使他们下去遭宰杀。他们有祸了，因为他们的日子，就是向他们追讨的时候，已经来到。 ###EN### Slay all her oxen; Let them go down to slaughter. Woe to them, for their day has come, The time of their punishment.
Verse_Ch: 50:28 有从巴比伦地逃跑脱身之人的声音，在锡安报告耶和华我们的神报仇，就是为祂的殿报仇。 ###EN### There is a sound of those who flee and escape From the land of Babylon, To declare in Zion The vengeance of Jehovah our God, The vengeance for His temple.
Verse_Ch: 50:29 要招集弓箭手，一切拉弓的人，攻击巴比伦；要在她四围安营攻击她；不要容一人逃脱。要照她所作的报应她；她怎样待人，也要怎样待她；因为 她敌对耶和华以色列的圣者，举动狂傲。 ###EN### Summon archers against Babylon, All those who bend the bow. Encamp against her all around; Let there be no escape. Recompense her according to her work; According to all that she has done, so do to her. For she has acted proudly against Jehovah, Against the Holy One of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 50:30 所以她的少年人，必仆倒在宽阔处；当那日，她一切的兵丁必默默无声；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### Therefore her young men will fall in her open squares, And all her men of war will be silenced in that day, Declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 50:31 主万军之耶和华说，你这狂傲的阿，我与你反对；因为你的日子，就是我向你追讨的时候，已经来到。 ###EN### Indeed, I am against you, O Pride, Declares the Lord Jehovah of hosts; For your day has come, The time that I visit you.
Verse_Ch: 50:32 狂傲的必绊跌仆倒，无人扶起。我也必使火在他的城邑中着起，将他四围所有的尽行烧灭。 ###EN### And Pride will stumble and fall, And there will be no one to raise him up. And I will kindle a fire in his cities, And it will devour all that is around him.
Verse_Ch: 50:33 万军之耶和华如此说，以色列人和犹大人一同受欺压；凡掳掠他们的，都紧紧抓住他们，不肯释放。 ###EN### Thus says Jehovah of hosts, The children of Israel And the children of Judah are oppressed together; And all who took them captive held them fast; They refused to let them go.
Verse_Ch: 50:34 他们的救赎主大有能力；万军之耶和华是祂的名。祂必为他们伸冤，好使这地得安息，却使巴比伦的居民扰乱不安。 ###EN### Their Redeemer is strong; Jehovah of hosts is His name. He will surely plead their cause, That He may give rest to the land But trouble to the inhabitants of Babylon.
Verse_Ch: 50:35 耶和华说，有刀剑攻击迦勒底人和巴比伦的居民，并她的首领和智慧人。 ###EN### The sword is against the Chaldeans, declares Jehovah, And against the inhabitants of Babylon And against her princes and against her wise men.
Verse_Ch: 50:36 有刀剑攻击说谎的人，他们就成为愚昧；有刀剑攻击她的勇士，他们就惊惶。 ###EN### The sword is against the liars, and they will become fools; The sword is against her mighty men, and they will be dismayed.
Verse_Ch: 50:37 有刀剑攻击他们的马匹、战车、和其中一切混杂的人民，他们必像妇女一样。有刀剑攻击她的财宝，那些财宝就被抢夺。 ###EN### The sword is against their horses and against their chariots And against all the mingled people who are in her midst, And they will become like women. The sword is against her treasuries, And they will be plundered.
Verse_Ch: 50:38 有干旱临到她的众水，众水就必干涸；因为这是有雕制偶像之地，人因可怕的偶像而癫狂。 ###EN### Drought is upon her waters, And they will dry up; For it is a land of graven images, And they are mad over terrifying idols.
Verse_Ch: 50:39 所以旷野的走兽和豺狼必住在那里，鸵鸟也住在其中。那里必永无居民，世世代代无人居住。 ###EN### Therefore desert animals will dwell there with hyenas, And ostriches will dwell in her. It will not be inhabited forever; It will not be dwelt in from generation to generation.
Verse_Ch: 50:40 耶和华说，必无人住在那里，也无世人在其中寄居，就像神所倾覆所多玛、蛾摩拉、和邻近的城邑一样。 ###EN### As when God overthrew Sodom And Gomorrah with its neighbors, Declares Jehovah, So no one will dwell there; Nor will a son of man sojourn in it.
Verse_Ch: 50:41 有一民从北方而来，并有一大国和许多君王被激动，从地极来到。 ###EN### A people is now coming from the north, And a great nation and many kings Are stirring from the uttermost parts of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 50:42 他们拿弓和枪，性情残忍，毫无怜悯。他们的声音，像海浪匉訇；巴比伦的女子阿，他们都骑马摆队，如上战场的人来攻击你。 ###EN### They grasp bow and spear; They are cruel and have no mercy. Their voice roars like the sea, And they ride upon horses, Set in array as a man for battle Against you, O daughter of Babylon.
Verse_Ch: 50:43 巴比伦王听见他们的风声，手就发软；痛苦将他抓住，疼痛仿佛正在生产的妇人。 ###EN### The king of Babylon has heard the report about them, And his hands are feeble; Distress has seized him, Pain like a woman in childbirth.
Verse_Ch: 50:44 必有一人像狮子从约但河边的丛林上来，攻击坚固的居所；转眼之间，我要使他们逃跑离开她；谁蒙拣选，我就派谁治理她。谁能像我呢？谁能给 我定规日期呢？谁是那能在我面前站立的牧人呢？ ###EN### Indeed, one will come up like a lion From the majesty of the Jordan against a secure habitation; For I will suddenly make them run away from her; And whoever is chosen I will appoint over her. For who is like Me? And who can appoint Me a time? And who is that shepherd who can stand before Me?
Verse_Ch: 50:45 所以你们要听耶和华攻击巴比伦所设的谋略，和祂攻击迦勒底人之地所定的意念：仇敌定要将他们羊群中微小的拉去；祂定要使他们的居所荒凉。 ###EN### Therefore hear the counsel of Jehovah, Which He purposed against Babylon, And His thoughts, which He has thought Against the land of the Chaldeans: Surely they will drag them off, the little ones of the flock; Surely He will make their habitation a desolation because of them.
Verse_Ch: 50:46 因巴比伦被占据的声音，地就震动，人在列邦都听见呼喊的声音。 ###EN### At the sound of Babylon being seized The earth trembles, And a cry is heard among the nations.
Chapter_Header: 51
Verse_Ch: 51:1 耶和华如此说，我必使毁灭的风刮起，攻击巴比伦和住在立加米的人。 ###EN### Thus says Jehovah, I will stir up against Babylon and against the inhabitants of Leb-kamai A destroying wind.
Verse_Ch: 51:2 我要打发外邦人攻击巴比伦，他们要簸扬她；在灾祸的日子，他们要周围攻击她，使她的地掳掠一空。 ###EN### And I will send strangers against Babylon, and they will winnow her, And they will empty her land When they come against her from every side In the evil day.
Verse_Ch: 51:3 弓箭手要向拉弓的和披甲挺身的射箭；不怜惜她的少年人，要灭尽她的全军。 ###EN### Against him who bends, let the archer bend his bow, And against him who stands up in his armor; And let them not spare her young men, But let them utterly destroy all her army.
Verse_Ch: 51:4 他们必在迦勒底人之地被杀仆倒，在巴比伦的街上被刺透。 ###EN### And they will fall down slain in the land of the Chaldeans And pierced through in her streets.
Verse_Ch: 51:5 以色列或犹大，并没有被他的神万军之耶和华遗弃；然而他们的地充满了违背以色列圣者的罪。 ###EN### For neither Israel or Judah is forsaken By his God, by Jehovah of hosts; But their land is full of guilt Against the Holy One of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 51:6 你们要从巴比伦中逃跑，各救自己的性命；不要在她的罪孽中被剪除，因为这是耶和华报仇的时候；祂必向巴比伦施行报应。 ###EN### Flee from the midst of Babylon, And let each man save his life; Do not be cut off in her iniquity; For this is a time of vengeance to Jehovah; He will give full recompense to her.
Verse_Ch: 51:7 巴比伦素来是耶和华手中的金杯，使全地沉醉；列国喝了她的酒就癫狂了。 ###EN### Babylon has been a golden cup in Jehovah's hand That has made all the earth drunk. The nations have drunk of her wine; Therefore the nations have become mad.
Verse_Ch: 51:8 巴比伦忽然倾覆毁坏；你们要为她哀号，拿乳香为她止痛，或者可以治好。 ###EN### Suddenly Babylon has fallen and become broken; Howl over her; Take balm for her pain, If perhaps she may be healed.
Verse_Ch: 51:9 我们本想医治巴比伦，她却没有治好。离开她罢，我们各人往本地去；因为她受的审判上达于天，高及云霄。 ###EN### We tried to heal Babylon, but she is not healed; Forsake her, and let each one of us go to his own land; For her judgment has reached to heaven And has been lifted up to the clouds.
Verse_Ch: 51:10 耶和华已经显出我们的公义；来罢，我们可以在锡安述说耶和华我们神的作为。 ###EN### Jehovah has brought forth our righteousnesses; Come and let us relate in Zion The work of Jehovah our God.
Verse_Ch: 51:11 你们要磨亮箭头，抓起盾牌。耶和华定意攻击巴比伦，要将她毁灭，就激动了玛代君王的灵，因这是耶和华的报仇，就是为祂的殿报仇。 ###EN### Polish the arrows, Take up the shields. Jehovah has stirred up the spirit of the kings of the Medes, because His purpose is against Babylon, to destroy her; for this is the vengeance of Jehovah, the vengeance for His temple.
Verse_Ch: 51:12 你们要竖立旌旗，攻击巴比伦的城墙；要加强守望，派定守望者，设下埋伏；因为耶和华指着巴比伦居民所说的话，不仅定了意，也已经作成了。 ###EN### Lift up a standard against the walls of Babylon; Make the watch strong. Set the watchmen; Prepare the ambushers; For Jehovah has both purposed and done What He spoke against the inhabitants of Babylon.
Verse_Ch: 51:13 住在众水之上多有财宝的阿，你的结局到了，你不义之财的量满了。 ###EN### O you who dwell by many waters, Abundant in treasures, Your end has come, The measure of your unjust gain.
Verse_Ch: 51:14 万军之耶和华指着自己起誓，说，我必使敌人充满你，像蝗虫一样；他们必对你发出胜利的呐喊。 ###EN### Jehovah of hosts has sworn by Himself, I will surely fill you with men like locusts, And they will raise a shout of victory over you.
Verse_Ch: 51:15 耶和华用能力造作大地，用智慧建立世界，用聪明铺张诸天。 ###EN### It is He who made the earth by His power, Who established the world by His wisdom, And by His understanding He stretched out the heavens.
Verse_Ch: 51:16 祂一发声，空中便有多水激动；祂使云雾从地极上升；祂为雨造闪电，从祂府库中带出风来。 ###EN### When He utters His voice, there is a tumult of waters in the heavens, And He causes the vapors to rise from the ends of the earth; He makes lightning for the rain And brings forth wind from His treasuries.
Verse_Ch: 51:17 各人都愚蠢，毫无知识；各金匠都因自己雕制的偶像羞愧；他所铸的像是虚假的，其中并无气息。 ###EN### Every man is stupid, without knowledge; Every goldsmith is put to shame by his idol; For his molten image is falsehood, And there is no breath in them.
Verse_Ch: 51:18 这些都是虚无的，是迷惑人的作品；到讨罪的时候，必要灭亡。 ###EN### They are vanity, the work of delusion; At the time of their punishment they will perish.
Verse_Ch: 51:19 雅各的分不像这些；因祂是形成万有的，以色列也是祂产业的支派；万军之耶和华是祂的名。 ###EN### The Portion of Jacob is not like these; For He is the One who formed everything, And Israel is the tribe of His inheritance; Jehovah of hosts is His name.
Verse_Ch: 51:20 祂说，你是我的大锤，我争战的兵器；我要用你打碎列邦，用你毁灭列国， ###EN### He says, You are My hammer, My weapons of war; And with you I will shatter nations, And with you I will destroy kingdoms,
Verse_Ch: 51:21 用你打碎马和骑马的，用你打碎战车和坐在其上的， ###EN### And with you I will shatter the horse and his rider, And with you I will shatter the chariot and its rider,
Verse_Ch: 51:22 用你打碎男人和女人，用你打碎老年人和少年人，用你打碎少男和处女， ###EN### And with you I will shatter man and woman, And with you I will shatter old man and young, And with you I will shatter young man and virgin,
Verse_Ch: 51:23 用你打碎牧人和他的群畜，用你打碎农夫和他的一对牛，用你打碎省长和官长。 ###EN### And with you I will shatter the shepherd and his flock, And with you I will shatter the farmer and his yoke of oxen, And with you I will shatter governors and officials.
Verse_Ch: 51:24 耶和华说，我必在你们眼前，报复巴比伦人和迦勒底一切居民在锡安所行的诸恶。 ###EN### And I will repay Babylon And all the inhabitants of Chaldea With all their evil which they have done In Zion before your eyes, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 51:25 耶和华说，你这行毁灭的山，就是毁灭全地的山哪，我与你反对；我必向你伸手，将你从岩石辊下去，使你成为焚烧的山。 ###EN### Indeed, I am against you, O mountain of destruction, Declares Jehovah, Which destroys the whole earth; And I will stretch out My hand upon you And roll you down from the rocks And make you a burning mountain.
Verse_Ch: 51:26 人必不从你那里取石头为房角石，也不取石头为根基石；你必永远荒凉；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### And they will not take from you a stone for the corner Or a stone for the foundations; For you will be an eternal desolation, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 51:27 要在这地竖立旌旗，在各国中吹角，使列国预备攻击她；将亚拉腊、米尼、亚实基拿各国招来攻击她；又派军长来攻击她，使马匹上来如可怕的蝗 虫； ###EN### Lift up a standard in the land; Blow a trumpet among the nations; Prepare the nations against her; Summon against her the kingdoms of Ararat, Minni, and Ashkenaz; Appoint an officer against her; Bring up the horses like terrifying locusts.
Verse_Ch: 51:28 使列国和玛代君王、省长、一切官长、并他们所管全地的人，都预备攻击她。 ###EN### Prepare the nations against her, The kings of the Medes, Their governors and all their officials, And all the land of their dominion.
Verse_Ch: 51:29 地必震动而翻腾；因耶和华向巴比伦所定的旨意成立了，要使巴比伦之地荒凉，无人居住。 ###EN### And the land trembles and writhes, For the purposes of Jehovah against Babylon stand, To make the land of Babylon a waste, Without inhabitant.
Verse_Ch: 51:30 巴比伦的勇士止息争战，留在坚垒之中；他们的勇力衰败，好像妇女一样；巴比伦的住处有火着起；她的门闩都折断了。 ###EN### The mighty men of Babylon have ceased fighting; They remain in strongholds; Their might has failed; they have become like women. Her dwellings are on fire; her bars are broken.
Verse_Ch: 51:31 跑信的彼此相遇，送信的互相迎接，报告巴比伦王说，城的四方被攻取了； ###EN### Runner runs to meet runner, And messenger to meet messenger, To announce to the king of Babylon That his city has been captured from end to end.
Verse_Ch: 51:32 渡口被占据了，苇塘被火烧了，兵丁都惊慌了。 ###EN### And the crossing places have been seized, And they burn the marshes with fire, And the men of war are terrified.
Verse_Ch: 51:33 因为万军之耶和华以色列的神如此说，巴比伦的女子好像踹谷时的禾场，再过片时，她被收割的时候就到了。 ###EN### For thus says Jehovah of hosts, the God of Israel, The daughter of Babylon is like a threshing floor At the time when it is trodden; Yet a little while and the time of harvest will come to her.
Verse_Ch: 51:34 巴比伦王尼布甲尼撒吞灭了我，压碎了我，使我成为空的器皿；他像龙将我吞下，用我的美物充满他的肚腹，又将我洗除出去。 ###EN### Nebuchadrezzar the king of Babylon has devoured me; He has crushed me; He has made me an empty vessel; He has swallowed me up like a dragon; He has filled his stomach with my delicacies; He has washed me out.
Verse_Ch: 51:35 锡安的居民要说，愿我和我肉体所受的强暴，归与巴比伦！耶路撒冷人要说，愿流我们血的罪，归到迦勒底的居民！ ###EN### The violence done to me and my flesh be on Babylon! The inhabitant of Zion will say; And my blood be upon the inhabitants of Chaldea! Jerusalem will say.
Verse_Ch: 51:36 所以耶和华如此说，我必为你伸冤，为你报仇；我必使巴比伦的海枯竭，使她的泉源干涸。 ###EN### Therefore thus says Jehovah, I will indeed plead your cause And execute vengeance for you; And I will dry up her sea And make her fountain dry.
Verse_Ch: 51:37 巴比伦必成为乱堆，为野狗的住处，令人惊骇、嗤笑，无人居住。 ###EN### And Babylon will become a heap of ruins, A habitation of jackals, An astonishment and a hissing, Without inhabitant.
Verse_Ch: 51:38 他们在一起要像少壮狮子咆哮，像小狮子吼叫。 ###EN### They will roar together like young lions; They will growl like lions' whelps.
Verse_Ch: 51:39 他们火热的时候，我必为他们设摆酒席，使他们沉醉，好叫他们快乐，睡了长觉，永不醒起；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### When they are inflamed, I will set out their drink; And I will make them drunk, that they may be merry And sleep an eternal sleep And not wake up, declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 51:40 我必使他们像羊羔，像公绵羊和公山羊，下到宰杀之地。 ###EN### And I will bring them down like lambs to the slaughter, Like rams with male goats.
Verse_Ch: 51:41 示沙克何竟被攻取！全地所称赞的，何竟被占据！巴比伦在列国中，何竟令人惊骇！ ###EN### How Sheshach has been captured, And the praise of all the earth seized! How Babylon has become an astonishment Among the nations!
Verse_Ch: 51:42 海水涨起，漫过巴比伦；她被许多海浪遮盖。 ###EN### The sea has come up over Babylon; She is covered with the multitude of its waves.
Verse_Ch: 51:43 她的城邑成为荒场、旱地、沙漠，无人居住、无人经过之地。 ###EN### Her cities have become a waste, A dry land and a desert, A land in which no one dwells, Through which no person passes.
Verse_Ch: 51:44 我必惩罚巴比伦的彼勒，使他吐出所吞的；列国必不再流归他那里；巴比伦的城墙也必坍塌。 ###EN### And I will punish Bel in Babylon And bring what he has swallowed out of his mouth; And the nations will not stream unto him any longer; Even the wall of Babylon will fall down.
Verse_Ch: 51:45 我的民哪，你们要从她中间出来，各人拯救自己的性命，躲避耶和华的烈怒。 ###EN### Come out from the midst of her, My people, And let each man save his life From the burning anger of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 51:46 你们不要心惊胆怯，也不要因在这地所听见的风声惧怕；因为一年有风声传来，另一年又有风声传来，地上有强暴的事，官长攻击官长。 ###EN### And lest your heart faint And you become afraid at the report that will be heard in the land-For the report will come in one year; And after that a report in another year And violence in the earth, Ruler against ruler -
Verse_Ch: 51:47 因此，日子将到，我必惩罚巴比伦的偶像；她全地必然抱愧；她被杀的人，必在其中仆倒。 ###EN### Therefore indeed, days are coming, When I will punish the idols of Babylon; And her whole land will be put to shame, And all her slain will fall in her midst.
Verse_Ch: 51:48 天地和其中所有的，必因巴比伦欢呼；因为行毁灭的，要从北方来攻击她；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### And the heavens and the earth and all which is in them Will give a ringing shout over Babylon; For out of the north the destroyers will come against her, Declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 51:49 地上被杀的人怎样曾因巴比伦仆倒，照样巴比伦也必因以色列被杀的人仆倒。 ###EN### Babylon is also to fall for the slain of Israel, As all the slain of the earth have fallen for Babylon .
Verse_Ch: 51:50 你们逃脱了刀剑的人要快走，不要站住；要在远方记念耶和华，心中追想耶路撒冷。 ###EN### You who have escaped the sword, Go and do not stand still; Remember Jehovah from afar, And let Jerusalem come up in your heart.
Verse_Ch: 51:51 我们因听见辱骂就蒙羞，满面惭愧；因为外人进了耶和华殿的圣所。 ###EN### We have been put to shame, for we have heard reproach; Disgrace has covered our faces; For strangers have come Into the holy places of the house of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 51:52 耶和华说，因此日子将到，我必惩罚巴比伦的偶像；在她全地受伤的人必唉哼。 ###EN### Therefore indeed, days are coming, Declares Jehovah, When I will punish her idols, And throughout her land the wounded will groan.
Verse_Ch: 51:53 巴比伦虽升到天上，虽使她坚固的高处更坚固，但仍有行毁灭的从我到她那里；这是耶和华说的。 ###EN### Though Babylon mount up to the heavens, And though she fortify the height of her strength, Destroyers will come from Me to her, Declares Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 51:54 有哀号的声音从巴比伦出来，有大毁灭从迦勒底人之地发出！ ###EN### The sound of a cry from Babylon, And great destruction from the land of the Chaldeans!
Verse_Ch: 51:55 因耶和华正在毁灭巴比伦，使其中的大声灭绝。他们的波浪仿佛众水匉訇，他们的闹声已经响起。 ###EN### For Jehovah is destroying Babylon, And He will cause the loud voice to perish from her. And their waves roar like many waters; The noise of their voice is raised.
Verse_Ch: 51:56 因为行毁灭的临到巴比伦，她的勇士被捉住；他们的弓折断了；因为耶和华是施行报应的神，必定施行完全的报应。 ###EN### For a destroyer has come upon her, upon Babylon, And her mighty men are taken captive; Their bows are broken into pieces; For Jehovah is a God of recompense; He will repay in full.
Verse_Ch: 51:57 名为万军之耶和华的王说，我必使巴比伦的首领、智慧人、省长、官长和勇士，都沉醉；他们必睡长觉，永不醒起。 ###EN### And I will make her princes and her wise men drunk, Her governors and her officials and her mighty men; And they will sleep an eternal sleep And not wake up, declares the King, Whose name is Jehovah of hosts.
Verse_Ch: 51:58 万军之耶和华如此说，巴比伦宽阔的城墙，必光秃赤露，她高大的城门必被火焚烧；众民必徒然劳碌，列国所劳碌的必被火焚烧；他们都必困乏。 ###EN### Thus says Jehovah of hosts, The broad walls of Babylon will be utterly laid bare; Her high gates will be burned with fire. So the peoples will have labored in vain; And the nations, only for fire; and they will have wearied themselves.
Verse_Ch: 51:59 犹大王西底家在位第四年，去巴比伦的时候，玛西雅的孙子，尼利亚的儿子西莱雅与王同去；(西莱雅是行宫总管；)申言者耶利米有话吩咐他。 ###EN### The word which Jeremiah the prophet commanded Seraiah the son of Neriah, the son of Mahseiah, when he went with Zedekiah the king of Judah to Babylon in the fourth year of his reign. (Now Seraiah was quartermaster.)
Verse_Ch: 51:60 耶利米将一切要临到巴比伦的灾祸，就是论到巴比伦的一切话，都写在书上。 ###EN### And Jeremiah wrote in a book all the evil that would come on Babylon, even all these words that are written concerning Babylon.
Verse_Ch: 51:61 耶利米对西莱雅说，你到了巴比伦，务要念这书上的话； ###EN### And Jeremiah said to Seraiah, When you come to Babylon, see that you read all these words;
Verse_Ch: 51:62 又说，耶和华阿，你曾论到这地方，说，要将其剪除，甚至连人带牲畜没有在这里居住的，必永远荒凉。 ###EN### And say, O Jehovah, You have spoken concerning this place, to cut it off, so that nothing should dwell in it, neither man nor animal, for it will be an eternal desolation.
Verse_Ch: 51:63 你念完了这书，就把一块石头拴在书上，扔在伯拉河中， ###EN### And as soon as you have finished reading this book, you shall bind a stone to it and cast it into the midst of the Euphrates,
Verse_Ch: 51:64 说，巴比伦因耶和华所要降与她的灾祸，必如此沉下去，不再兴起，人民也必困乏。耶利米的话到此为止。 ###EN### And say, Thus Babylon will sink and will not rise up because of the evil which I will bring upon it, and they will weary themselves. Thus far are the words of Jeremiah.
Chapter_Header: 52
Verse_Ch: 52:1 西底家登基的时候年二十一岁，在耶路撒冷作王十一年；他母亲名叫哈慕他，是立拿人耶利米的女儿。 ###EN### Zedekiah was twenty-one years old when he began to reign, and he reigned eleven years in Jerusalem; and his mother's name was Hamutal, the daughter of Jere- miah, from Libnah.
Verse_Ch: 52:2 西底家行耶和华眼中看为恶的事，是照约雅敬一切所行的。 ###EN### And he did what was evil in the sight of Jehovah, according to all that Jehoiakim had done.
Verse_Ch: 52:3 这些事临到耶路撒冷和犹大，是因耶和华的怒气发作，直到祂将人民从自己面前赶出。后来西底家背叛了巴比伦王。 ###EN### For it was through the anger of Jehovah that this came to pass in Jerusalem and Judah until He cast them out from His presence. And Zedekiah rebelled against the king of Babylon.
Verse_Ch: 52:4 他作王第九年十月初十日，巴比伦王尼布甲尼撒率领全军来攻击耶路撒冷，对城安营，四围筑垒攻城。 ###EN### And in the ninth year of his reign, in the tenth month, on the tenth of the month, Nebuchadrezzar the king of Babylon came, he and his whole army, against Jerusalem and encamped against it; and they built a siege wall against it all around.
Verse_Ch: 52:5 于是城被围困，直到西底家王十一年。 ###EN### So the city came under siege until the eleventh year of King Zedekiah.
Verse_Ch: 52:6 四月初九日，城里饥荒严重，甚至那地的百姓都没有粮食。 ###EN### In the fourth month, on the ninth day of the month, the famine was so severe within the city that there was no food for the people of the land.
Verse_Ch: 52:7 城被攻破，一切兵丁就在夜间从靠近王园两城墙之间的门，出城逃跑，迦勒底人正在四围攻城，他们沿着通往亚拉巴的路逃去。 ###EN### Then the city was breached, and all the men of war fled; and they went out from the city by night by way of the gate between the two walls, which was by the king's garden, while the Chaldeans were all around the city; and they went by the way toward the Arabah.
Verse_Ch: 52:8 迦勒底人的军队追赶西底家王，在耶利哥的平原追上他；他的全军都离开他四散了。 ###EN### And the army of the Chaldeans pursued after the king, and they overtook Zedekiah in the plains of Jericho; and all his army was scattered from him.
Verse_Ch: 52:9 迦勒底人拿住王，带他到在哈马地利比拉的巴比伦王那里；巴比伦王便审判他。 ###EN### And they seized the king and brought him up to the king of Babylon at Riblah in the land of Hamath, and he pronounced judgments on him.
Verse_Ch: 52:10 巴比伦王在西底家眼前杀了他的众子，又在利比拉杀了犹大的一切首领； ###EN### Then the king of Babylon slaughtered the sons of Zedekiah before his eyes, and he also slaughtered all the princes of Judah at Riblah.
Verse_Ch: 52:11 并且剜了西底家的眼睛，用铜链锁着他。巴比伦王将他带到巴比伦去，把他囚在监里，直到他死的日子。 ###EN### And he put out Zedekiah's eyes and bound him with bronze fetters. And the king of Babylon brought him to Babylon and put him in prison until the day of his death.
Verse_Ch: 52:12 巴比伦王尼布甲尼撒十九年五月初十日，在巴比伦王面前侍立的护卫长尼布撒拉旦来到耶路撒冷， ###EN### And in the fifth month, on the tenth day of the month (this was the nineteenth year of King Nebuchadrezzar, the king of Babylon), Nebuzaradan, the captain of the bodyguard, who stood before the king of Babylon, came to Jerusalem.
Verse_Ch: 52:13 焚烧耶和华的殿和王宫，并耶路撒冷一切的房屋；每一大幢的房屋，他都用火焚烧了。 ###EN### And he burned the house of Jehovah and the king's house and all the houses of Jerusalem, and every large house he burned with fire.
Verse_Ch: 52:14 跟从护卫长的迦勒底人全军，就拆毁耶路撒冷四围的城墙。 ###EN### And all the army of the Chaldeans who were with the captain of the bodyguard broke down all the walls around Jerusalem .
Verse_Ch: 52:15 那时护卫长尼布撒拉旦将民中最穷的，和城里所余剩的百姓，并已经投降巴比伦王的人，以及所余剩的群众，都迁徙去了。 ###EN### And the poor of the people and the rest of the people who were left in the city and the deserters who deserted to the king of Babylon and the rest of the multitude, Nebuzaradan the captain of the bodyguard carried away into exile.
Verse_Ch: 52:16 但护卫长尼布撒拉旦留下那地一些最穷的人，使他们修理葡萄园，耕种田地。 ###EN### But Nebuzaradan the captain of the bodyguard left some of the poorest of the land to be vinedressers and field workers.
Verse_Ch: 52:17 耶和华殿的铜柱，并耶和华殿的盆座和铜海，迦勒底人都打碎了，将所有的铜运到巴比伦去。 ###EN### And the Chaldeans broke in pieces the bronze pillars, which were in the house of Jehovah, and the bases and the bronze sea, which were in the house of Jehovah. And they carried all their bronze to Babylon.
Verse_Ch: 52:18 他们又把锅、铲、灯剪、盘子、调羹、并供职用的一切铜器，都带去了。 ###EN### And they took away the pots and the shovels and the snuffers and the basins and the spoons and all the bronze vessels with which they ministered.
Verse_Ch: 52:19 杯、火盆、盘子、锅、灯台、调羹、壶，无论金的银的，护卫长也都带去了。 ###EN### And the captain of the bodyguard took away the dishes and the firepans and the basins and the pots and the lampstands and the spoons and the bowls, that which was of gold: for its gold, and that which was of silver, for its silver.
Verse_Ch: 52:20 所罗门为耶和华殿所造的两根铜柱、一个铜海、并座下的十二只铜牛，这一切器物的铜，多得无法可称。 ###EN### As for the two pillars, the one sea, and the twelve bronze oxen, which were under the bases, which King Solomon made for the house of Jehovah, the bronze of all these vessels was beyond weight.
Verse_Ch: 52:21 这一根柱子高十八肘，围十二肘，厚四指，当中是空的。 ###EN### And as for the pillars, the height of one pillar was eighteen cubits, and it was twelve cubits in circumference, and it was four fingers in thickness; it was hollow.
Verse_Ch: 52:22 柱上有铜的柱顶，高五肘，柱顶的周围有网子和石榴，都是铜的；那一根柱子，照此一样，也有石榴。 ###EN### And a bronze capital was upon it; and the height of each capital was five cubits; and the network and pomegranates were upon the capital all around, all of bronze; and the second pillar and the pomegranates were like these.
Verse_Ch: 52:23 柱子四面有九十六个石榴；在网子周围，共有一百个石榴。 ###EN### And there were ninety-six pomegranates on the four sides; all the pomegranates on the network were a hundred all around.
Verse_Ch: 52:24 护卫长拿住祭司长西莱雅、副祭司西番亚、和三个守门的； ###EN### And the captain of the bodyguard took Seraiah the chief priest and Zephaniah the second priest and the three doorkeepers.
Verse_Ch: 52:25 又从城中拿住一个管理兵丁的太监，并在城里所遇常见王面的七个人，和检点那地人民之军长的书记，以及城里所遇见那地的民六十个人。 ###EN### And from the city he took one eunuch, who was overseer of the men of war, and seven men from the king's inner circle who were found in the city, and the scribe of the captain of the army, who mustered the people of the land, and sixty men of the people of the land who were found in the midst of the city.
Verse_Ch: 52:26 护卫长尼布撒拉旦将这些人带到在利比拉的巴比伦王那里。 ###EN### And Nebuzaradan the captain of the bodyguard took them and brought them to the king of Babylon in Riblah.
Verse_Ch: 52:27 巴比伦王就击杀他们，在哈马地的利比拉把他们处死。这样，犹大人被迁徙离开了本地。 ###EN### And the king of Babylon struck them down and put them to death in Riblah, in the land of Hamath; so Judah was carried away into exile out of its land.
Verse_Ch: 52:28 尼布甲尼撒所迁徙的人民，记在下面；在他第七年有犹大人三千零二十三名。 ###EN### These are the people whom Nebuchadrezzar carried into exile: in the seventh year, three thousand and twenty- three Jews;
Verse_Ch: 52:29 尼布甲尼撒十八年从耶路撒冷迁徙去八百三十二人。 ###EN### In the eighteenth year of Nebuchadrezzar, eight hundred and thirty-two persons from Jerusalem;
Verse_Ch: 52:30 尼布甲尼撒二十三年，护卫长尼布撒拉旦迁徙去犹大人七百四十五人；共有四千六百人。 ###EN### In the twenty-third year of Nebuchadrezzar, Nebuzaradan the captain of the bodyguard carried from the Jews seven hundred and forty-five persons into exile. There were four thousand six hundred persons in all.
Verse_Ch: 52:31 犹大王约雅斤被迁徙后三十七年，就是巴比伦王以未米罗达登基那一年，十二月二十五日，巴比伦王使犹大王约雅斤抬头，提他出监； ###EN### And in the thirty-seventh year of the exile of Jehoiachin the king of Judah, in the twelfth month, on the twenty-fifth of the month, Evil-merodach the king of Babylon, in the year that he became king, released Jehoiachin the king of Judah and brought him out of prison.
Verse_Ch: 52:32 又对他说恩慈的话，使他的位高过与他一同在巴比伦众王的位。 ###EN### And he spoke with him kindly and set his throne above the thrones of the kings who were with him in Babylon.
Verse_Ch: 52:33 他换下囚服，终身常在巴比伦王面前吃饭。 ###EN### And Jehoiachin changed his prison garments and ate his food before him continually all the days of his life.
Verse_Ch: 52:34 他所需用的食物，不断由巴比伦王赐给，每日一分，终身都是这样，直到他死的日子。 ###EN### And for his allowance, a continual allowance was given to him by the king of Babylon, a portion for each day, all the days of his life until the day of his death.
